# Plate package Slate v2 migration

Objective:
Migrate Plate packages to Slate v2 package-by-package; done when all in-scope owners pass focused proof or are deferred with owner, and apps/www playground works.

Goal plan:
docs/plans/2026-06-20-plate-package-slate-v2-migration.md

Template:
docs/plans/templates/slate-migration.md

Primary template:
docs/plans/templates/slate-migration.md

Applied packs:
- none

Migration source:
- type: user-directed `$auto` routed to `slate-migration`
- prompt / link: current thread
- migration surface: Plate packages that still depend on `@platejs/slate-legacy`
  or stale Slate/Plate legacy APIs
- source owner: current Slate v2 packages in this checkout:
  `packages/slate`, `packages/slate-dom`, `packages/slate-react`,
  `packages/slate-history`, `packages/slate-hyperscript`, `packages/yjs`,
  and `packages/browser`
- target owner: Plate packages, app playground/docs/examples, and any migration
  helper scripts created for this lane
- invocation mode: full-loop, package-by-package
- completion threshold summary: every migrated package owner passes its focused
  build/typecheck/test proof before the next owner starts; final `apps/www`
  playground proof passes; no changesets are created for this beta lane

First checkpoint:
- Before implementation or broad exploration, copy every explicit prompt
  requirement into this plan as checkable rows: scope, owners, non-goals,
  timing, stop conditions, deliverables, migration-guide expectations,
  changeset expectations, verification surfaces, and final handoff sections.
- Do not continue into implementation until this extraction is complete or
  explicitly marked N/A with reason.

Completion threshold:
- Inventory identifies all current Plate owners importing `@platejs/slate-legacy`
  or stale Slate v1-ish APIs, and ranks them in a safe package-by-package order.
- For each owner in the active migration order, move to the next package only
  after focused owner proof passes: build when applicable, typecheck, tests, and
  browser/example proof when the package affects `apps/www` editor behavior.
- Stale imports, fake aliases, old augmented API assumptions, unnecessary legacy
  glue, and dead Slate compatibility paths are cut or logged as deferred with
  owner and exact reason.
- Migration helper scripts/tooling may be added when they reduce risk,
  duplicate work, or proof friction; helper output must be durable and scoped.
- No changesets are created or required for this lane so Slate beta packages can
  release without coupling to Plate package beta release notes.
- Future Plate v2 notes are collected as suggestions/artifacts, not used as a
  reason to block this migration.
- `apps/www` playground/editor route proof works after the migrated package
  slice.
- Migration closure is legal only when inventory, API map, stale-symbol audit,
  source/docs/examples/tests, migration guide decisions, changeset decisions,
  packet ledger, changed list, review-attention rows, stopping checkpoints, and
  final verification evidence are complete or explicitly deferred with owner,
  and `node .agents/skills/autogoal/scripts/check-complete.mjs docs/plans/2026-06-20-plate-package-slate-v2-migration.md`
  passes.

Verification surface:
- Source audits: package import graph for `@platejs/slate-legacy`, old Slate
  package imports, old `T*` generics/augmented API patterns, and migration
  hotspots.
- Package proof: `pnpm turbo typecheck --filter=./packages/<owner>`;
  `pnpm --filter @platejs/<owner> test` or the package-local test script;
  package build when the package ships artifacts or the package proof uses dist.
- App proof: `pnpm --filter www typecheck` or equivalent source-first app proof
  after app-visible migration; Browser proof on `apps/www` playground/editor
  route before final handoff.
- Slate substrate proof when a package crosses raw Slate behavior:
  `pnpm check:slate:fast` or a focused Slate package/browser row.
- Final mechanical proof:
  `node .agents/skills/autogoal/scripts/check-complete.mjs docs/plans/2026-06-20-plate-package-slate-v2-migration.md`.

Constraints:
- Current transplanted Slate source in this Plate checkout beats memory and old
  plans.
- Patch source owners, not generated mirrors or caller glue, unless the caller
  is the owner.
- Remove stale aliases and fake compat paths instead of preserving bad API
  shape.
- Repair migration guide and changesets during the loop when gaps appear.
- Do not create commits, PRs, or pushes unless explicitly requested.
- Do not create changesets for this migration lane.
- Do not migrate the whole Plate runtime blindly. One owner/package slice at a
  time; next slice waits for proof.
- Preserve Slate/Plate boundary: do not pollute Slate substrate with Plate
  product concerns, and do not hide Slate primitive gaps in Plate glue.
- Prefer hard cuts over compatibility aliases/shims.
- Keep public docs latest-state; migration notes may use before/after language
  only when they are explicit migration docs.

Boundaries:
- Source of truth: current Plate repo checkout and transplanted Slate v2
  packages; old donor checkout is not proof authority.
- Allowed edit scope: migration plan/artifacts, scoped helper scripts/tooling,
  package owners selected by the active packet, focused docs/migration notes
  when a missing user-facing step is proven, and app playground proof fixes.
- Migration guide owner: `content/docs/slate/migration.mdx` or the current
  migration docs route only when a real user-facing migration step is missing.
- Changeset owner: N/A for this lane by explicit user instruction.
- Package/API owners: current package slice only; no next package until focused
  proof passes or packet is reverted/quarantined.
- Browser/example surfaces: `apps/www` playground/editor routes; exact route to
  be selected after inventory finds the first app-visible migrated owner.
- Non-goals: npm publish, PR creation, Plate v2 public redesign, release
  notes/changesets, broad pagination, broad Slate runtime architecture work.

Output budget strategy:
- Use inventory scripts/artifacts for repo-wide import and symbol scans instead
  of streaming broad `rg` output.
- Exclude generated/build/cache paths by default:
  `node_modules`, `.next`, `.turbo`, `dist`, `coverage`, `test-results`,
  transplant archives unless explicitly auditing ledger truth.
- Prefer `rg --files`, package manifest parsing, import graph scripts, and
  counts before inspecting individual owner files.
- Store migration inventory under `docs/plans/artifacts/plate-slate-v2-migration/`.

Blocked condition:
- Block only when the next migration slice requires an unsafe public API/runtime
  fork not covered by `VISION.md`, a user-only product/taste decision, external
  credentials, commit/PR/push authority, or when no package can be migrated or
  deferred without destroying behavior.

Migration state:
- surface: Plate packages using Slate legacy/stale APIs
- mode: full-loop package-by-package
- minimum_runtime: N/A, no duration requested
- current_loop: 333
- current_checkpoint: foundation legacy-import retirement
- current_checkpoint_status: done; direct core source imports are isolated to
  `packages/core/src/internal/currentRuntimeBridge.ts`, scanner classifies that
  bridge as private quarantine, and focused core proof is green
- next_checkpoint: hard pause before full Plate runtime/default-route swap,
  `packages/slate-legacy` deletion, public Plate v2 API redesign, or any
  deferred runtime owner claim
- goal_status: active

Foundation migration checkpoint (2026-06-22):
- [x] Scope copied before code edits: foundation migration first.
- [x] Requirement copied before code edits: keep packages green.
- [x] Requirement copied before code edits: remove `@platejs/slate-legacy`
      imports where they are not the explicit temporary runtime boundary.
- [x] Requirement copied before code edits: add temporary private bridges only
      where needed.
- [x] Requirement copied before code edits: do not expose temporary bridges as
      final public API.
- [x] Non-goal copied before code edits: do not design or hard-cut the whole
      Plate v2 public API in this packet.
- [x] Stop condition copied before code edits: if a remaining legacy import is
      tied to current runtime construction, history/react enhancer behavior,
      editor API/transform contracts, or plugin override semantics, either move
      it behind a private core bridge with focused proof or defer it to the
      runtime/default-route checkpoint with owner and reason.
- [x] Inventory all current non-generated `@platejs/slate-legacy` references.
      Evidence: `rg -n "from '@platejs/slate-legacy'" packages apps content
      docs --glob '!docs/plans/**'` reports only the private core bridge and
      `packages/slate-legacy` type tests.
- [x] Remove or privatize safe foundation imports package-by-package. Evidence:
      core constructor/type/history/plugin-resolution imports now route through
      `packages/core/src/internal/currentRuntimeBridge.ts`.
- [x] Run focused core/package proof after each kept packet. Evidence: core
      typecheck, core tests, core build, migration scanner, and command-surface
      scanner are green.
- [x] Record keep/revert/quarantine plus remaining deferred owner rows.
      Evidence: loop 334 addendum and `hit-overrides.json` private bridge row.

Current verdict:
- verdict: package-by-package migration lane was closed, but foundation
  legacy-import retirement is reopened as a narrow checkpoint; broad Plate
  runtime/default-route migration remains a separate hard checkpoint
- confidence: 99/100 after safe package packets, first-party app playground proof,
  source-backed runtime adapter map, kept runtime factory packet, and kept
  plugin metadata/configuration/API-capability packets, plus command-surface
  inventory for every `extendApi` / transform / editor-mutation owner,
  source-backed transform-to-tx design, first runtime tx registration proof,
  plugin authoring DSL for tx groups, tx-backed Plate command facades,
  first package mark-toggle tx family, first package block-toggle tx family,
  the basic-style `set` command family, code-block toggle command family, and
  classic todo-list item toggle command family, plus current-runtime execution
  proof for tx-backed facades, comment mark/node command family, command
  inventory repair that separates spec fixtures, core command facades, clean
  runtime-backed API capabilities, and legacy batch/history transforms from simple tx candidates, selection
  duplicate-block insertion tx proof, and typed Plate `editor.update` inference
  for selection document transforms and select command proof; tests no longer
  hide `editor.update((tx) => ...)` inference behind `tx: any`; AI
  replayable node/mark transforms now use `editor.update` and AI command
  facades are classified as mixed instead of raw simple-tx debt; core
  `editor.tf.setValue` now uses `tx.value.replace`; existing migrated
  tx-backed facades no longer use `(editor as any).update((tx: any) => ...)`,
  basic-nodes now proves inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx[plugin.key].*)`
  from plugin `extendTx` metadata, and the command-surface scanner recognizes
  typed generic update calls as tx-backed facades instead of stale raw transform
  candidates; `HistoryPlugin` keeps the current-runtime legacy `withHistory`
  wrapper as an explicit typed bridge instead of a double `as any`;
  `packages/list-classic` now makes its current-runtime legacy
  helper boundary explicit instead of relying on aggregate `platejs` helper
  leaks, `packages/code-block` no longer imports `@platejs/slate-legacy` or
  declares direct `slate` / `slate-dom` dependencies after replacing child
  traversal and legacy fixture creation with direct node-shape / Plate fixture
  setup, `packages/basic-nodes` no longer imports `@platejs/slate-legacy` after
  replacing its blockquote spec node lookup with `editor.api.node`, and
  `packages/list-classic` manifests declare their temporary legacy scaffold
  dependencies honestly; `init` now uses Slate v2 `Selection` / `Value` types,
  explicit `createPlateEditor({ runtime: 'slate-v2' })` supports `rootPlugin`
  configuration and root/plugin `decorate` through a real root plugin parent,
  and `AnyPluginConfig.tx` is now a typed object-shaped metadata slot instead
  of `any`, with runtime plugin input widened only at the generic inference
  boundary;
  and the attempted `tx.value.replace` initialization rewrite is quarantined
  because it fired startup operations and broke existing init/node-id/on-change
  behavior; React provider hook/store/test-helper type surfaces now use
  `@platejs/slate` structural types where typecheck proves they are not tied to
  legacy runtime construction; React editor entrypoints use Slate v2 `Value`
  while leaving the legacy `Editor/createEditor` constructor explicit in
  `withPlate`; remaining React structural `Value` references in `pipeOnChange`
  and editor type specs are migrated, while render-leaf `NodeApi` is confirmed
  runtime-bound and stays legacy until `PlateEditor` is a v2 editor; core
  plugin/static/render decorator vocabulary now uses Slate v2 `Element` /
  `Text` / `Range` / operation/value types, with only current Plate runtime API
  surfaces left on legacy; editor type roots now use Slate v2 `Value`,
  `Range`, and `Selection` while legacy operation/editor-base/API/transform
  contracts stay quarantined until the runtime constructor moves; the temporary
  current-runtime update bridge now uses a typed `EditorUpdateTransaction`
  boundary plus `EditorUpdateContext`, and the runtime proof exercises
  `editor.update<PluginTx<...>>()` directly instead of a transaction cast helper;
  the future `createPlateRuntimeEditor` path now mounts under the actual
  `@platejs/slate-react` `<Slate>` provider, exposes the same editor through v2
  hooks, and dispatches `onValueChange` from `editor.update`; the
  `createPlateRuntimeEditor` scaffold/spec now have no local `any` casts or
  `PlateRuntimeEditor<any, any>` aliases, with unresolved plugin metadata
  editor access held at `unknown`; `PlateRuntimeSlate` now gives the v2 runtime
  path a real Plate-owned provider adapter that wraps `@platejs/slate-react`
  `<Slate>` and applies Plate `aboveSlate` render wrappers without the old
  `initialValue` facade; `PlateRuntimeEditable` now proves the v2 runtime path
  can mount `@platejs/slate-react` `<Editable>` with Plate-owned
  `beforeEditable`, `aboveEditable`, `afterEditable`, `renderEditable`, and
  plugin `useHooks` execution under the wrapped editable branch; `PlateRuntimeContent`
  now composes the v2 provider and editable adapters into one internal content
  entrypoint while preserving value/extension generic typing and Slate
  callbacks; old `PlateContent` store/effect behavior is now isolated behind
  `PlateContentEffects` / `PlateContentStateEffect` and covered by focused
  contract tests for read-only store sync, node/text handler sync, and
  autofocus-on-editable, without replacing old `PlateContent` yet; `packages/mention`,
  `packages/basic-styles`, `packages/basic-nodes`, `packages/date`,
  `packages/tag`, `packages/math`, `packages/callout`, and `packages/media`
  now import raw Slate transaction typing from `@platejs/slate` directly instead
  of hiding it behind aggregate `platejs`
- next owner: core runtime/helper-boundary retirement checkpoint; legacy
  `withPlate` route no longer hides the `withSlate` options handoff behind raw
  `any`
- keep / revert / quarantine call: `packages/table` traversal helper migration
  kept; table now uses Slate v2 `NodeApi`, `PathApi`, `RangeApi`, and `TextApi`
  where behavior is structural, while keeping legacy `InsertNodesOptions`,
  `SetNodesOptions`, `EditorAboveOptions`, `At`, and `combineTransformMatchOptions`
  because those are still current Plate transform/API option contracts.
  `packages/list` legacy dependency removal
  kept; list now uses Slate v2 `NodeApi.getIf` / `PathApi` with explicit
  `hasPrevious` guards instead of relying on legacy `PathApi.previous`
  returning undefined. `packages/table`
  explicit runtime-helper boundary kept; v2 `PathApi.previous` replacement in
  table previous-cell helpers rejected because behavior proof showed throwing
  drift; legacy `PathApi.previous` kept there until the runtime helper semantics
  are replaced deliberately. `PlateRuntimeEditable` adapter kept;
  `PlateRuntimeContent` adapter kept; `PlateContentEffects` isolation kept;
  `PlateRuntimeSlate` adapter kept; v2 provider mount proof kept; latest
  current-runtime update bridge type cleanup kept; React adapter boundary
  artifact kept; render-leaf `NodeApi` swap
  quarantined
- reason: the internal v2 runtime factory can now carry basic Plate plugin
  metadata, configuration/functional extension metadata, and plugin-specific API
  capabilities through Slate v2 extensions without owning properties on the
  `editor.api` proxy; option-state API callbacks now write through the installed
  runtime plugin options store instead of a stale pre-install metadata object;
  command-surface inventory proves transforms mostly close
  over legacy `editor.tf`; plugin authors can now use `extendTx(...)` to
  install Slate v2 tx groups, and the new runtime scaffold no longer overrides
  Slate v2 `editor.getApi`; `packages/basic-nodes` mark toggles now use
  `extendTx(...)` plus a typed `extendTransforms(...)` facade backed by
  `editor.update((tx) => tx[plugin.key].*)`; its heading/blockquote toggles now
  use inline tx groups instead of the over-extracted `createBlockToggleTx`
  helper; `packages/basic-styles` now exposes `set(...)` command facades backed
  by tx groups instead of `addMark` / `setNodes`; `packages/code-block` now
  exposes its code-block toggle through an inline tx group plus the same
  tx-backed facade; `packages/list-classic` todo-list item toggle now exposes
  an inline tx group plus the same tx-backed facade. Current `withSlate`
  installs a temporary legacy update bridge so tx-backed facades execute under
  the current Plate runtime while the full Slate v2 runtime migration continues;
  core proof now uses local fixtures instead of importing product plugins.
  Remaining work is raw command families, initialization, React provider
  behavior, and the aggregate public Plate surface. `packages/list-classic`
  wrapper-list toggles are not safe to wrap blindly because they are complex
  selection/range/list-structure algorithms; they are deferred to the list tx
  operation/runtime owner instead of becoming fake tx facades. `nodeId.normalize`
  is also not a simple tx candidate because it owns `withoutSaving` +
  `setNodesBatch` history/batch behavior under the current legacy runtime.
  `packages/selection` duplicate selected blocks now routes the replayable
  document insertion through `editor.update((tx) => tx.nodes.insert(...))`,
  while selected-id plugin state stays outside tx as a UI side effect. The
  interim Plate editor types now expose Slate v2 `EditorUpdateTransaction`, so
  package transform code gets inferred `tx` instead of `(editor as any).update`.
  Remaining broad `any` around `update` is quarantined inside the temporary
  current-runtime legacy bridge, not package transforms or proof call sites.
  `packages/ai` now has zero raw transform rows: simple AI insert/remove/unset
  commands are tx-backed, while preview/history/chat/copilot commands are
  classified as mixed/runtime surfaces because they own batching, focus, async
  state, or fragment algorithms. `setValue` is the first initialization
  subpacket moved to `tx.value.replace`; full `init` is intentionally not
  rewritten yet because it owns async value loading, HTML string deserialize,
  selection, initial transforms, normalization, and `onReady`. The user called
  out that tx-backed facades still used broad update casts, so the migration
  first introduced a typed `PluginTx<K, Group>` scaffold, then moved
  basic-nodes to inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx[plugin.key].*)` through
  plugin `extendTx` metadata. The temporary current-runtime bridge now lives in
  `legacyRuntimeUpdateBridge.ts`. The scanner now treats
  `.update<PluginTx<...>>()` as an editor update call, so typed migrations keep
  the inventory honest instead of being reclassified as raw transform debt.
  `init` still owns lifecycle-specific direct value/selection assignment under
  the current legacy runtime because replacing it with the current tx bridge
  caused real startup operations; this is runtime architecture debt, not a
  package-local facade migration. The React provider safe slice moved hooks,
  stores, and test helpers off legacy structural types; remaining React legacy
  imports are concentrated in `withPlate`, `PlateEditor`, Plate plugin/runtime
  typing, fallback editor, and render-leaf/onChange utilities. `withPlate`,
  `usePlateEditor`, and `usePlateViewEditor` now accept v2 `Value` generics,
  but `withPlate` still constructs/enhances a legacy `Editor` until the runtime
  swap packet. `pipeOnChange` and editor type specs now use v2 `Value`; render
  leaf utilities still use legacy `NodeApi` because v2 `NodeApi.get` requires a
  v2 editor runtime shape that current `PlateEditor` does not implement. The
  latest bridge cleanup does not make the legacy runtime a full Slate v2
  transaction runtime; it narrows the unsafe surface to an explicit bridge
  boundary and keeps package/plugin call sites on typed `editor.update`.
  React adapter inspection proves a direct `slate-react` re-export swap would
  be fake compatibility because v2 `Slate` does not expose the old
  `initialValue` contract and v2 has `createReactEditor` instead of `withReact`.
  The v2 Plate runtime scaffold now exposes the same generic
  `update<PluginTx<...>>()` typing as the current-runtime Plate editor bridge,
  and its focused spec no longer uses a tx cast helper. Its plugin metadata
  model also owns `useHooks` directly instead of discovering it through a cast,
  and its installed plugin registry is now typed instead of `unknown`.

Completion rule:
- Do not call `update_goal(status: complete)` while any required checklist item
  remains unchecked. If an item does not apply, check it and add
  `N/A: <reason>`.
- Do not call `update_goal(status: complete)` until every completion threshold
  above is satisfied, final handoff evidence is recorded, and
  `node .agents/skills/autogoal/scripts/check-complete.mjs docs/plans/2026-06-20-plate-package-slate-v2-migration.md`
  passes.
- Do not create hook state for this goal. This file plus the active goal are
  the durable state.

| 154 | update | migration-packet, proof, stale-symbol-audit | `packages/core` TPlateEditor spec fixture split | `TPlateEditor.spec.ts` imported legacy `createEditor` only to seed Plate editor type/API assertions. | kept; spec now uses package-owned `createPlateEditor` fixtures and core proof is green |
| 155 | update | migration-packet, proof, stale-symbol-audit | `packages/core` withStatic spec fixture split | `withStatic.spec.tsx` imported legacy `createEditor` only to pass an already-created editor into static editor tests. | kept; existing-editor cases now use package-owned `createSlateEditor` fixtures and core proof is green |
| 156 | update | migration-packet, proof, stale-symbol-audit | `packages/core` affinity live text lookup helper split | `AffinityPlugin` used legacy `NodeApi.get` only to read current and next text nodes at editor-owned paths. | kept; live lookups now use `editor.api.node(path)?.[0]` and affinity proof is green |
| 157 | update | migration-packet, proof, stale-symbol-audit | `packages/core` chunking current-root predicate split | Chunking needed a default current-editor-root predicate, not the whole legacy `NodeApi` surface; previous v2 `NodeApi.isEditor` attempt failed on current Plate roots. | kept; local current-runtime root predicate is covered by an oracle and core proof is green |
| 158 | update | stale-symbol-audit, api-map, stopping-checkpoint | `packages/core` remaining legacy runtime boundary quarantine | Remaining core legacy imports are constructor/editor API/history/operation/plugin-contract surfaces, not safe helper swaps. | artifact added; next work should either start a deliberate core runtime packet or move to the next non-core package owner |
| 159 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | tx group transaction boundary typing and `packages/basic-nodes` inline tx proof | User challenged `(editor as any).update((tx: any) => ...)` and the endgame for inferred tx types. The remaining weakness was that `PlatePluginTxGroup` accepted `unknown`, forcing plugin tx groups to cast the transaction locally even after `editor.update` inference was fixed. | kept; `PlatePluginTxGroup` now receives `EditorUpdateTransaction`, basic-nodes mark/heading/blockquote tx groups use the typed transaction boundary, `createBlockToggleTx` remains absent, and basic-nodes/core proof is green |
| 160 | update | inventory, stale-symbol-audit, api-map, migration-packet, proof, workflow-slowdown | scanner legacy-symbol repair, app comparison quarantine, docs guide cleanup, and `packages/callout` insert option owner | Broad app/docs checks exposed two kinds of false/real debt: intentional upstream Slate comparison imports should not be migrated, while removed aggregate option/helper exports were not all visible to the stale-symbol scanner. | kept; scanner now detects stale aggregate option/helper names and supports quarantined hit overrides, docs guide snippets no longer teach stale imports/types, app comparison rows are quarantined, and callout derives insert options from the current Plate facade with package proof green |
| 161 | update | migration-packet, proof, stale-symbol-audit, workflow-slowdown | `packages/media` insert/set option owner and aggregate fixture repair | Media had stale aggregate insert/set option imports in lib/react insertion surfaces; package proof also exposed an old aggregate `createEditor` fixture that now resolves to Slate v2 after the hard cut. | kept; media derives current-runtime insert/set option aliases from `SlateEditor['tf']` / `PlateEditor['tf']`, option-bag casts are removed, the image embed spec uses package-owned Plate editor construction, and media proof is green |
| 178 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` initial-value transform parity | The v2 runtime scaffold cached `transformInitialValue` plugins but did not execute them, so initialization parity would silently miss NodeId/table-style startup transforms once Plate routes through the v2 runtime. | kept; runtime scaffold now executes current `transformInitialValue` hooks after plugin metadata installation, skips read-only editOnly transforms, rejects undefined returns, and keeps `normalizeInitialValue` out of the v2 runtime path |
| 179 | update | api-map, stopping-checkpoint | `create-plate-editor-v2-routing-readiness.md` | A public `createPlateEditor` runtime swap would be fake green while default Plate core plugins still depend on global editor APIs/transforms, `overrideEditor`, legacy React/history enhancers, and apply wrappers. | kept; routing artifact names blockers and orders the next packets, starting with Debug API, History, React enhancer, SlateReactExtension keyboard/reset, DOM/apply, callback pipelines, and override rules |
| 180 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` global editor API support | `DebugPlugin`-style global `extendEditorApi` is a safe Slate v2 extension API packet; rejecting it kept an easy default-core blocker alive without improving safety. | kept; runtime scaffold now installs non-transform global editor APIs through `defineEditorExtension({ api })`, while global transforms and overrides still throw; focused runtime proof covers `editor.api.debug.*` without proxy own-property mutation |
| 181 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` HistoryPlugin v2 route | Default Plate `HistoryPlugin` still carries legacy `withHistory`, but the v2 runtime already installs Slate v2 `history()` through `createReactEditor`; layering the legacy enhancer would be wrong. | kept; runtime plugin normalization strips the legacy `extendEditor` only for the `history` route, v2 history is proven with `tx.text.insert` + `tx.history.undo`, and the attempted duplicate `createReactEditor({ history: false })` API was cut in favor of existing `history({ enabled: false })` preset disabling |
| 182 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` ReactPlugin legacy enhancer route | Default Plate `ReactPlugin` still carries legacy `withReact`, but the v2 runtime already installs Slate v2 `react()` through `createReactEditor`; preserving the legacy enhancer would layer two React runtimes. | kept; runtime plugin normalization strips legacy `extendEditor` for the `dom` route, proof shows `ReactPlugin` now stops on DOM global API/transform/runtime behavior instead of `uses extendEditor`, and the next owner is the DOM runtime packet |
| 183 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` DOM runtime packet | Default Plate `DOMPlugin` still exposed global scroll APIs/transforms and `overrideEditor(apply)` wrappers for auto-scroll and previous-selection bookkeeping, while Slate v2 expects extension API plus operation middleware. | kept; runtime plugin normalization maps DOM transform metadata into the Plate transform facade, installs a v2 `plate:dom:runtime` extension for `scrollIntoView`, auto-scroll operation targeting, and `set_selection` bookkeeping, and removes the circular legacy `SlateEditor` type dependency from `AUTO_SCROLL` / `withScrolling` |
| 184 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `SlateReactExtensionPlugin` keyboard/reset runtime packet | Default Plate `SlateReactExtensionPlugin` inherits `SlateExtensionPlugin` metadata and owns keyboard shortcuts plus reset/focus behavior; rejecting the inherited global transforms blocked `ReactPlugin` from mounting under the v2 runtime route. | kept; runtime plugin normalization skips the old global SlateExtension transform/override metadata for this scaffold, installs typed root keyboard handlers through `PlateRuntimeEditable`, and exposes a v2 reset transform that replaces the root value through inferred `editor.update((tx) => ...)` while restoring focus through the React API bridge |
| 185 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `SlateExtensionPlugin` callback/apply runtime packet | The legacy `SlateExtensionPlugin` `apply` wrapper owned onNodeChange/onTextChange state capture around node/text operations; the v2 runtime needs that behavior as operation middleware, not as a legacy global transform wrapper. | kept; `createPlateRuntimeEditor` installs a Slate v2 `operations.apply` extension for SlateExtension node/text callbacks, reads before/after node state from the v2 value snapshot with primary-root normalization, and proves configured callbacks fire for `tx.nodes.set(...)` and `tx.text.insert(...)` |
| 186 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `SlateExtensionPlugin` setValue runtime packet | `setValue` is a replayable value replacement and should not stay behind the skipped legacy global transform metadata in the v2 runtime scaffold. | kept; `editor.tf.setValue(value)` now routes through `tx.value.replace({ children })`, empty values use the runtime default paragraph, and string HTML values require an installed `api.html.deserialize` capability instead of a fake parser |
| 187 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `SlateExtensionPlugin` resetBlock runtime packet | `resetBlock` is a focused node-property command that can run through v2 node transactions instead of the skipped legacy global transform metadata. | kept; runtime `editor.tf.resetBlock` finds an explicit or selection-derived element path, preserves the configured id key, unsets non-structural element props, and sets the paragraph type through v2 `tx.nodes.unset` / `tx.nodes.set` |
| 188 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map, workflow-slowdown | `SlateExtensionPlugin` liftBlock runtime packet | `liftBlock` is a focused block unwrap command that can run through v2 node transactions instead of the skipped legacy global transform metadata. | kept; runtime `editor.tf.liftBlock` finds an explicit or selection-derived block path, requires a matching ancestor, and unwraps through typed v2 `tx.nodes.unwrap` |
| 189 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `SlateExtensionPlugin` insertExitBreak runtime packet | `insertExitBreak` is a focused insertion command that can run through v2 node transactions instead of the skipped legacy global transform metadata. | kept; runtime `editor.tf.insertExitBreak` inserts a default block before or after the target ancestor, preserves strict-sibling ancestor targeting, and selects the inserted block through v2 `tx.nodes.insert` |
| 190 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `SlateExtensionPlugin` init lifecycle runtime packet | `init` is startup/lifecycle value loading, not a plain user `setValue`; it needed a v2 route that avoids direct `children` mutation while preserving transform/selection/onReady semantics. | kept; runtime `editor.tf.init` resolves direct/async values, skips history on replacement, runs runtime `transformInitialValue`, preserves selection through transform passes, optionally normalizes, and calls `onReady` with the final readable value |
| 191 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `SlateReactExtensionPlugin` memo cleanup / override behavior packet | The remaining SlateReact override was the `_memo` cleanup normalizer; keeping it as skipped override metadata would make the v2 runtime scaffold accept memoized editable values it should clean. | kept; runtime plugin normalization now installs a Slate v2 `normalizers.node` extension that removes `_memo` through `tx.nodes.unset(...)` and stops that pass, matching the old override behavior without a fake `normalizeNode` facade |
| 192 | update | migration-packet, proof, api-map | `OverridePlugin` schema element-spec packet | `withOverrides` is the schema/API slice of `OverridePlugin`; plugin node flags need to become Slate v2 element specs before break/delete/merge/normalize wrappers can be ported honestly. | kept; runtime metadata now registers Slate v2 element specs from Plate plugin node flags (`isInline`, `isVoid`, `isMarkableVoid`, `isSelectable`) and proves schema predicates through `state.schema.*`; transform wrappers remain blocked owners |
| 305 | update | migration-packet, proof, stale-symbol-audit, workflow-slowdown | `SlateExtensionPlugin` v2 OperationApi classifier bridge | The old quarantine row was stale after the v2 runtime callback route landed; direct v2 `OperationApi` import works only when the current-runtime apply callback is treated as a structural boundary instead of letting TypeScript infer the old legacy operation subtype. | kept; `SlateExtensionPlugin` imports `OperationApi` from `@platejs/slate`, introduces typed `NodeOperation` / `TextOperation` locals after v2 guards, passes those typed operations into node/text handler pipes, removes the stale scanner override, and records the proof/dist-refresh slowdown |
| 306 | update | migration-packet, proof, workflow-slowdown | SlateExtension node/text handler pipe context typing | `pipeOnNodeChange`, `pipeOnTextChange`, and `isElementStateEmpty` duplicated local `as any` plugin-context bridges even though `getEditorPlugin` already owns that current-runtime context boundary. | kept; pipe utilities and metadata-prop checks now derive typed handler/context aliases from `AnyEditorPlugin`, spread `getEditorPlugin(editor, plugin)`, and keep the only unresolved plugin-context bridge inside `getEditorPlugin` |
| 307 | update | proof, app-proof, stopping-checkpoint | apps/www playground migrated-state proof | The routing readiness artifact named playground proof as the next order before any default runtime flip. | kept; current migrated package state is proven in `/blocks/playground` through `www` typecheck and focused Chromium edit/undo/redo proof; next owner is the hard runtime/default-route decision |
| 308 | update | migration-packet, proof, workflow-slowdown | `createPlateEditor({ runtime: 'slate-v2' })` root initialization options | The explicit v2 route still rejected sync initialization options that the runtime can support without legacy shims, keeping default-route readiness artificially worse. | kept; v2 `createPlateEditor` now accepts root `transformInitialValue`, `autoSelect`, `shouldNormalizeEditor`, and sync `onReady`, while still rejecting async/string values, `skipInitialization`, `rootPlugin`, render/handler/component root options, and other broad legacy-only root config |
| 309 | update | migration-packet, proof, workflow-slowdown | `createPlateEditor({ runtime: 'slate-v2' })` root render wrappers | The explicit v2 route still rejected root `render` even though `PlateRuntimeSlate` / `PlateRuntimeEditable` already consume wrapper render slots. | kept; v2 `createPlateEditor` now carries root `render.aboveSlate`, `render.aboveEditable`, `render.beforeEditable`, and `render.afterEditable` through the synthetic root runtime plugin; node component `components`, `render.node`, and root `handlers` stay rejected until separate adapter proof |

| Old API / pattern | Slate v2 target | Owner | Evidence | Status |
|-------------------|-----------------|-------|----------|--------|
| `TElement` / `TText` imported from `@platejs/slate-legacy` | `Element` / `Text` from `@platejs/slate` for package-local base types | `packages/utils` | `packages/utils/src/lib/plate-types.ts`, hooks, placeholder plugin | kept |
| `TextApi`, `ElementApi`, `PathApi`, `NodeApi.getIf` primitives | import from `@platejs/slate` where package only needs substrate primitives | `packages/utils`, `packages/table` | `SingleLinePlugin`, `withNormalizeTypes`, `withTrailingBlock`, table spec | kept |
| `RenderElementProps`, `RenderTextProps`, `RenderLeafProps`, static render props, node-data attribute helpers | import `Element`, `Text`, `Path`, `LeafPosition` from `@platejs/slate` and DOM primitive types from `@platejs/slate-dom` | `packages/core` | Core primitive packet: render/static types, node-data helpers, `getPlainText` | kept |
| Parser/injection fragment helpers | import `Descendant`, `Element`, `Text`, `Path`, `ElementApi`, `TextApi` from `@platejs/slate` where behavior is structural | `packages/core` | `pipeInjectNodeProps`, `pluginInjectNodeProps`, insert/transform fragment helpers/specs, HTML deserialize helpers | kept |
| React/static render node components | import `Element`, `Text`, `Path` from `@platejs/slate` for component props and static render prop helpers | `packages/core` | `react/components/plate-nodes.tsx`, `static/components/slate-nodes.tsx`, `static/utils/getRenderNodeStaticProps.ts` | kept |
| Selected Point/Path/Element hook and helper types | import structural `Point`, `Path`, `Element`, `NodeEntry`, `Descendant`, operations from `@platejs/slate` where callers do not pass legacy editor as a v2 root | `packages/core` | input rules, navigation, element store hooks/spec, selected DOM fragment, normalize descendants, on-node/text-change pipes | kept |
| `queryNode` / `QueryNodeOptions` | Plate-owned structural helper exported by `@platejs/core` | `packages/core` | Added `packages/core/src/lib/utils/queryNode.ts`; consumed by core node-id and utils trailing-block | kept |
| Package-local `TElement` extension type | `Element` from `@platejs/slate` when the package defines its own element data shape | `packages/basic-nodes` | `BaseBlockquotePlugin` and `BaseCodeDrawingPlugin` pattern; first owner migrated and proven | in_progress |

| Plate runtime factory scaffold | internal `createPlateRuntimeEditor` over `@platejs/slate-react` `createReactEditor` plus Plate-owned identity/meta/cache state, plus internal `PlateRuntimeSlate` / `PlateRuntimeEditable` / `PlateRuntimeContent` adapters over v2 React components | `packages/core` | `packages/core/src/react/editor/createPlateRuntimeEditor.ts`, `packages/core/src/react/editor/createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts`; focused core proof green through provider, editable wrapper, and combined content adapters | kept |

| Plate runtime focus transform | core `editor.tf.focus({ at, edge, retries })` facade over Slate v2 selection + DOM focus | `packages/core` | Runtime scaffold resolves `startEditor` / `endEditor` / `at+edge` against the v2 root value, sets selection through `editor.update((tx) => tx.selection.set(...))`, and calls the v2 DOM focus capability; focused spec proves edge selection semantics | kept |
| PlateContent v2 state effect mount | `PlateContentStateEffect` depends on a minimal state editor contract, so old `PlateContent` and new `PlateRuntimeContent` can share the same read-only/callback/autofocus effect proof | `packages/core` | `PlateContent.spec.tsx` mounts `PlateRuntimeContent` under `PlateStoreProvider` with `PlateContentStateEffect`, verifies store read-only sync, `SlateExtensionPlugin` option sync, and `tf.focus({ edge: 'endEditor' })` after read-only flips off | kept |
| Plate plugin metadata on v2 runtime | legacy-free plugin flattening, dependency order, overrides, option stores, shortcuts, component/cache metadata, and explicit unsupported command-surface errors | `packages/core` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` supports simple plugin records and rejects editor mutation until owning packets migrate those contracts | kept |
| Plate plugin configuration on v2 runtime | resolve `configure()`, functional `.extend(...)`, configured input-rule arrays, and nested `configurePlugin(...)` with a v2-safe context | `packages/core` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` resolves config metadata before plugin registration and still rejects `extendEditor` / editor api-transform mutation after config resolution | kept |
| Plate runtime initial value transforms | execute current `transformInitialValue` plugins after v2 runtime plugin metadata installation; do not add old `normalizeInitialValue` compatibility to the v2 runtime path | `packages/core` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` pipes the current root value through plugin `transformInitialValue` hooks, honors read-only `editOnly.transformInitialValue`, throws on undefined returns, and replaces the v2 root value through `editor.update((tx) => tx.value.replace(...))` with focused proof | kept |
| Plate HistoryPlugin v2 route | strip legacy `extendEditor: withHistory` only in `createPlateRuntimeEditor`; rely on Slate v2 `history()` installed by `createReactEditor` | `packages/core` / `packages/slate-react` | `HistoryPlugin` still owns `withPlateHistory` for the current legacy public runtime, but the v2 runtime scaffold normalizes that plugin before support checks and proves `tx.text.insert` + `tx.history.undo` behavior through Slate v2 history | kept |
| Plate ReactPlugin v2 route | strip legacy `extendEditor: withReact` only in `createPlateRuntimeEditor`; rely on Slate v2 `react()` installed by `createReactEditor` | `packages/core` / `packages/slate-react` | `ReactPlugin` still owns `withPlateReact` for the current legacy public runtime, but the v2 runtime scaffold normalizes the `dom` plugin route before support checks; proof shows remaining failure is DOM global API/transform/apply behavior, not the legacy React enhancer | kept |
| Plate DOMPlugin v2 runtime route | global `extendEditorApi` / `extendEditorTransforms` / `overrideEditor(apply)` becomes a narrow runtime bridge: Slate v2 extension API for `scrollIntoView`, Plate transform facade for `withScrolling`, and operation middleware for auto-scroll plus `set_selection` bookkeeping | `packages/core` / `packages/slate-dom` / `packages/slate-react` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` handles only the DOM plugin metadata shape: `withScrolling` toggles `AUTO_SCROLL` and option overrides without a legacy `SlateEditor` type dependency; `plate:dom:runtime` installs `scrollIntoView`, tracks enabled scroll operations, and updates `editor.dom.prevSelection` / `currentKeyboardEvent`; arbitrary global transform/override plugins remain blocked | kept |
| Plate SlateReactExtension keyboard/reset v2 route | root keydown handlers pipe through `PlateRuntimeEditable`; reset becomes a Slate v2 value replacement plus selection clear and focus restore, not a legacy global transform wrapper | `packages/core` / `packages/slate-react` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now recognizes inherited `slateExtension` transform metadata as a deliberate skip for the runtime scaffold, installs no-op root shortcut commands plus typed keydown handler piping, and implements `editor.tf.reset()` through inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx.value.replace(...))` / `tx.selection.clear()` with React focus state routed through `editor.api.react.isFocused()` | kept; old callback/apply pipeline and memo cleanup remain separate owners |
| Plate SlateExtension callback pipeline v2 route | legacy `apply` callback capture becomes Slate v2 `operations.apply` middleware for node/text operations; command transforms remain separate | `packages/core` / `packages/slate` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` installs `plate:slate-extension:runtime`, captures previous/current nodes around `set_node` and text before/after around `insert_text`, calls plugin handler pipes first, then configured `onNodeChange` / `onTextChange`; internal operation root `main` is normalized to an omitted public root read key | kept |
| Plate SlateExtension setValue v2 route | root `editor.tf.setValue` becomes a v2 root-value replacement; string HTML remains an explicit HTML API capability | `packages/core` / `packages/slate` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` exposes `setValue(value)` on the runtime transform facade; array values and empty/default values call `editor.update((tx) => tx.value.replace(...))`, while string values call `editor.api.html.deserialize` only when that capability is installed | kept |
| Plate SlateExtension resetBlock v2 route | root `editor.tf.resetBlock` becomes v2 node unset/set operations over an explicit or selection-derived element path | `packages/core` / `packages/slate` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` resolves the target element path from `at` or selection, preserves the node-id key, removes extra element props with `tx.nodes.unset`, and sets the paragraph type with `tx.nodes.set<SlateElement>` | kept |
| Plate SlateExtension liftBlock v2 route | root `editor.tf.liftBlock({ at, match })` becomes a v2 unwrap operation over an explicit or selection-derived block target | `packages/core` / `packages/slate` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` resolves the target block, requires a matching ancestor, and unwraps through `tx.nodes.unwrap<SlateElement>` with the same object/function match predicate | kept |
| Plate SlateExtension insertExitBreak v2 route | root `editor.tf.insertExitBreak({ at, match, reverse })` becomes a v2 insert operation over the explicit or selection-derived block target | `packages/core` / `packages/slate` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` requires a collapsed selection unless `at` is explicit, finds the nearest ancestor that accepts paragraph siblings unless a match overrides it, inserts the configured default paragraph before/after the target with `tx.nodes.insert`, and uses `ElementOrTextIn<V>` so the inserted block remains tied to the editor value type | kept |
| Plate SlateExtension init v2 route | root `editor.tf.init(...)` becomes a lifecycle value replacement route with history skipped and transform/selection/onReady semantics preserved | `packages/core` / `packages/slate` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` resolves direct and async values, deserializes strings through the installed HTML API, falls back to the current value or runtime default paragraph, applies selection or auto-selection, runs runtime `transformInitialValue`, preserves selection across transform passes, runs explicit normalize only when requested, and calls `onReady` with the final readable root | kept |
| Plate plugin API capabilities on v2 runtime | plugin-specific `extendApi(...)` becomes Slate v2 extension `api` capability instead of owned properties on the proxy | `packages/core` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` registers plugin APIs through `defineEditorExtension({ api })`; Plate plugin APIs are read through `getPluginApi(plugin)` so raw Slate keeps `getApi(extension)`; transforms stay blocked | kept |
| Plate plugin-state API capabilities | Plate-facing helper/state API remains a Plate plugin API capability when it does not mutate the Slate document or hide a runtime override | `packages/link` / migration tooling | `LinkPlugin` `editor.api.link.getAttributes` only binds a helper over link attributes, while `editor.api.floatingLink` only updates plugin option state; scanner classifies both as `plate-plugin-state-api-capability` and focused link proof stays green | kept |
| Export side-effect API/transform facades | export/download APIs and facades read editor value or trigger host/browser side effects; they are not replayable Slate tx groups | `packages/docx-io` / migration tooling | `DocxExportPlugin` `exportToBlob` reads the current value/component overrides and `download` triggers browser download side effects; `exportAndDownload` composes those APIs. Scanner classifies them as `export-side-effect-api-capability` and `export-side-effect-transform-facade` after focused docx proof. | kept |
| Deferred runtime owners | current-runtime package behavior stays green, but v2 runtime parity is broad enough to need a dedicated behavior owner before claiming support | `packages/ai`, `packages/suggestion`, `packages/table`, `packages/selection`, `packages/media`, `packages/list-classic`, migration tooling | `BaseAIPlugin`, `AIChatPlugin`, and `CopilotPlugin` own AI preview/history, streaming markdown insertion, chat state/API, block selection integration, completion/cancel flows, and copilot debounce/abort/suggestion side effects. `BaseSuggestionPlugin` wraps insertText, deleteBackward/Forward, deleteFragment, insertBreak, insertFragment, insertNodes, normalizeNode, removeMark, removeNodes, plus suggestion API queries/state toggles. `BaseTablePlugin` exposes table create/query APIs, row/column/table insert/delete transforms, merge/split transforms, and `withTable` table selection/paste/delete/normalize/key-navigation behavior. `BlockSelectionPlugin` and `CursorOverlayPlugin` own DOM selection/cursor state, block-selection APIs, selected-id state, keyboard movement, copy/paste helpers, and block-selection transform facades. `BaseImagePlugin` and `PlaceholderPlugin` own upload/embed/drop/paste/history/plugin-state side effects around `withImageUpload`, `withImageEmbed`, `insertImageFromFiles`, `insertMedia`, `writeHistory`, and `uploadingFiles`. `BaseListPlugin` owns nested classic list normalization, paste, delete, indent/outdent, selection-unhang, and wrapper toggle algorithms; standalone classic todo `action_item` insertBreak is runtime-backed and the todo toggle remains tx-backed. Focused package proof is green for all deferred owners, and scanner classifies their broad runtime rows as `deferred-runtime-owner` instead of raw tx debt. | deferred-with-owner |
| Plate plugin command surface | owner-ranked migration ledger for `extendApi`, `extendEditorApi`, `extendTransforms`, `extendEditorTransforms`, `overrideEditor`, and `extendEditor` | `packages/core` plus package owners | `scan-plate-command-surface.mjs` now finds 312 rows across 30 owners and separates accepted tx-backed facades, Plate plugin-state API, export side-effect API/transforms, core command facades, legacy batch/history transforms, test fixtures, runtime-backed owners, mixed runtime owners, and raw transform debt; `packages/link` and `packages/docx-io` have 0 open command rows | inventory kept; next raw command/runtime family pending |
| Plate transform-to-tx design | replayable mutations become Slate v2 tx groups; host/runtime side effects stay API capabilities; editor interception maps to middleware/normalizers/operations/setup | `packages/core` | `core-transform-to-tx-design.md` source-audits Slate v2 `EditorUpdateTransaction` / `EditorExtensionTxGroup` and current Plate `extendTransforms` / `editor.tf` ownership | design/runtime/dsl kept; package transform pending |
| Plate runtime tx registration | plugin-owned tx groups are registered as Slate v2 extension `tx`, executed only inside `editor.update` | `packages/core` | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` accepts plugin `tx` groups, installs them through `defineEditorExtension({ tx })`, and tests full-document replacement through `tx.value.replace({ children })` | kept |
| Plate plugin tx authoring and command facade | `extendTx(...)` stores plugin tx group factories; tx-backed `extendTransforms(...)` remains the typed Plate facade for beta; `getTransforms(plugin)` / `editor.tf` return that facade | `packages/core` | `createSlatePlugin`, `toPlatePlugin`, and React/Slate plugin types expose `extendTx`; `createPlateRuntimeEditor` resolves `__txExtensions`, registers plugin-specific transform facades, and proves both raw tx and facade calls mutate through `editor.update` | kept; first package transform family kept |

Changed list:
- code/runtime/API: `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now recognizes first-party
  classic todo `action_item` override metadata and routes collapsed start/end
  `insertBreak` through Slate v2 node transactions, preserving classic checked
  inheritance options and selecting the inserted line-end item.
- tests/oracles: `BaseTodoListPlugin.spec.ts` now proves the standalone classic
  todo insertBreak route through public `createPlateEditor({ runtime:
  'slate-v2' })`, removes private `__txExtensions` broad-cast proof, and keeps
  nested `ul/ol/li/lic` list behavior deferred.
- tooling/proof: command-surface inventory now marks `BaseTodoListPlugin`
  override as `runtime-backed-editor-decision`; `packages/list-classic` still
  has five deferred nested classic list rows.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now codifies the explicit
  Slate v2 root boundary: top-level `api` and `transforms` stay rejected on
  `createPlateEditor({ runtime: 'slate-v2' })`; plugin APIs/transforms remain
  available through `getPluginApi(plugin)` / `getTransforms(plugin)`.
- code/runtime/API: `createPlateEditor({ runtime: 'slate-v2', shortcuts })`
  now accepts root shortcuts, carries them on the runtime root plugin, and mounts
  `EditorHotkeysEffect` inside `PlateRuntimeEditable` so shortcuts bind to the
  actual Slate v2 editable root.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/slate-react` `Editable` now exposes a public ref
  contract for the contenteditable root and composes it with the virtualized
  DOM-strategy root ref instead of overwriting non-virtualized refs.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` proves root shortcut hotkeys
  bind and invoke the handler on a Slate v2 runtime editor; `editable-behavior`
  proves `<Editable ref>` points at `[data-slate-editor]`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/caption` now stringifies caption fragments through a local `stringifyCaption(...)` helper backed by Slate v2 `NodeApi.isNode` / `NodeApi.string`, removing the production fake-parent `as any` stringification cast.
- code/runtime/API: `withCaption` remains an explicit runtime override owner because it wraps `apply` / `moveLine` and mutates caption focus option state; it is not a replayable tx command facade.
- tests/proof: caption package test/typecheck/lint/build are green, and command-surface inventory still classifies caption as `editor-runtime-decision`.

- code/runtime/API: runtime `editor.tf.insertFragment(fragment, options)` inserts through Slate v2 `tx.fragment.insert(...)`; parser fragment output is narrowed at this transaction boundary instead of widened to `any` or routed through legacy `editor.tf.insertFragment`.
