- code/runtime/API: runtime normalize rules now remove empty element targets only when the effective Plate normalize rule says `removeEmpty: true`; match overrides can force or veto the rule.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves normalize remove-empty, default keep, match-force, and match-veto behavior with block-level fixtures that avoid unrelated child-shape normalization noise.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now consumes the `OverridePlugin` merge wrapper on the v2 runtime route through Slate v2 query and operation middleware.
- code/runtime/API: runtime merge rules now preserve Plate behavior for `merge.removeEmpty`: pure paragraph-like blocks can remove empty previous targets, custom blocks keep the previous target by default, and match overrides can veto removal while preserving target props.
- code/runtime/API: the preserved empty-target path rewrites Slate v2 structural cleanup from `remove_node` into placeholder-child cleanup plus `merge_node`, avoiding a fake legacy editor facade.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves merge remove-empty, custom-target default keep, and match-override veto behavior; the first failing proof caught the prop-preservation gap before the final fix.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now consumes the `OverridePlugin` delete wrapper on the v2 runtime route while leaving normalize as the remaining OverridePlugin behavior owner.
- code/runtime/API: runtime `editor.tf.deleteBackward`, `deleteForward`, and `deleteFragment` now route through Slate v2 transactions and preserve Plate delete-rule behavior for reset/lift/full-document reset cases.
- code/runtime/API: runtime `editor.tf.reset({ children: true, select: true })` now selects the start of the reset document, which is needed for full-document delete.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves delete-rule start reset, empty reset, matched lift, default document-start reset, normal backward delete fallback, and full-document fragment reset.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now consumes the `OverridePlugin` schema and break override wrappers on the v2 runtime route while leaving normalize as a later behavior owner.
- code/runtime/API: runtime `editor.tf.insertBreak()` now applies Plate break rules through Slate v2 transactions: default structural break, empty reset, Plate `lineBreak` newline insertion, emptyLineEnd `deleteExit`, and `splitReset` continuation reset.
- code/runtime/API: runtime `editor.tf.insertSoftBreak()` preserves Plate facade semantics by inserting `\n`; this does not change Slate v2 `tx.break.insertSoft()`, which remains the raw Slate structural command.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves OverridePlugin break-rule behavior with a partial runtime override plugin so later delete/merge/normalize wrappers are not silently blessed.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now exposes `editor.tf.resetBlock({ at })` as v2 node transactions: resolve target element path, preserve id key, unset extra props, and set the paragraph type.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves runtime `resetBlock` works with explicit path and selection-derived target.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now maps `SlateReactExtensionPlugin` memo cleanup onto a Slate v2 `normalizers.node` extension instead of skipped legacy `overrideEditor(normalizeNode)` metadata.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves `_memo` markers are removed by forced normalization through the v2 runtime route.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now registers Slate v2 element specs from Plate plugin node schema flags (`isInline`, `isVoid`, `isMarkableVoid`, and `isSelectable`).
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves the resulting schema behavior through `state.schema.isInline`, `isVoid`, `markableVoid`, and `isSelectable`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now exposes `editor.tf.setValue(value)` as a v2 value replacement; empty values use the runtime default paragraph, and HTML strings require an installed `api.html.deserialize` capability.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves runtime `setValue` replaces the document and resets empty values to the default paragraph without legacy transform metadata.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now installs a SlateExtension operation middleware route for configured `onNodeChange` / `onTextChange` callbacks instead of relying on legacy `apply` wrapper semantics.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` runtime node/text callback capture reads before/after values from the Slate v2 value snapshot, including internal `main` root normalization before public primary-root reads.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves `SlateExtensionPlugin.configure({ options: { onNodeChange } })` fires for `tx.nodes.set(...)` and `onTextChange` fires for `tx.text.insert(...)`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now routes `SlateReactExtensionPlugin` keyboard behavior through `PlateRuntimeEditable` by piping plugin `onKeyDown` handlers before caller props, with typed handler context instead of `any`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` runtime `reset` now uses a v2 transaction path: `editor.update((tx) => tx.value.replace(...))`, `tx.selection.clear()`, and focus restoration through the React API bridge when the editor was focused.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` explicitly skips inherited `SlateExtensionPlugin` global transform/override metadata in the v2 runtime scaffold; remaining command transforms and memo cleanup stay blocked owners rather than fake-supported compatibility.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves SlateReact keydown routing calls the root movement command for `ArrowUp`, records `currentKeyboardEvent`, and proves runtime reset replaces the document with a default paragraph without local `tx: any`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now maps `DOMPlugin` onto a Slate v2 runtime bridge: DOM `withScrolling` lands in the Plate transform facade, `scrollIntoView` is installed through a `plate:dom:runtime` extension API, and auto-scroll / previous-selection bookkeeping run through operation middleware instead of legacy `overrideEditor(apply)`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` DOM auto-scroll state is no longer typed to the legacy `SlateEditor`; `AUTO_SCROLL` is object-keyed and `withScrolling` talks to a minimal `{ key: 'dom' }` option owner to avoid circular `typeof DOMPlugin` inference.
- tests/oracles: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` now proves `ReactPlugin` routes through DOM successfully, exposes `isScrolling` / `scrollIntoView`, toggles `withScrolling`, mutates through inferred `editor.update((tx) => ...)`, and clears `currentKeyboardEvent` while recording the previous selection on `set_selection`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now treats `ReactPlugin` as a v2-handled route for the legacy enhancer only: `extendEditor: withReact` is stripped for plugin key `dom`, and remaining DOM behavior is routed to the DOM runtime packet.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now treats `HistoryPlugin` as a v2-handled route: legacy `extendEditor: withHistory` is stripped only for plugin key `history`, while Slate v2 history comes from `createReactEditor` / `history()`.
- tests/oracles: runtime History proof now uses a saveable `tx.text.insert(...)` operation followed by `tx.history.undo()`; the rejected `createReactEditor({ history: false })` detour was removed in favor of the existing `history({ enabled: false })` preset-disabling contract.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now supports global editor API-only extensions such as `DebugPlugin` through Slate v2 extension APIs, while global transforms and overrides remain blocked.
- docs/plans/artifacts: added `create-plate-editor-v2-routing-readiness.md`, which blocks a premature `createPlateEditor` runtime swap and orders the global core runtime packets.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now executes current `transformInitialValue` plugins during v2 runtime editor creation, skips read-only editOnly transforms, throws on undefined transform returns, and keeps old `normalizeInitialValue` out of the v2 runtime path.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/ai` no longer imports aggregate `History`, `RemoveNodesOptions`, `EditorNodesOptions`, `NodeEntry`, `Path`, or `ElementApi` for the touched history/chat paths; option aliases derive from current `SlateEditor`/`PlateEditor` facades, and `@platejs/slate` is a real runtime dependency because AI imports Slate v2 structural APIs in emitted code.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/suggestion` no longer imports missing aggregate `getAt` / `combineMatchOptions` or stale aggregate node option/value helpers in the touched query/transform/plugin paths; Suggestion owns local node-to-location normalization and local query predicate composition, with Slate v2 `ElementApi` / `NodeApi` / `TextApi` structural checks.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/diff` no longer hides its current legacy mutable editor dependency behind aggregate `platejs` imports; `createEditor`, operation/editor-transform types, and `EditorApi['isInline']` come from explicit `@platejs/slate-legacy`, and package proof quarantines that boundary until the diff algorithm is rewritten around Slate v2 transactions.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/code-drawing` `insertCodeDrawing` options now derive from `SlateEditor['tf']['insertNodes']` through exported `InsertCodeDrawingOptions`; stale aggregate `InsertNodesOptions` is gone.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/date` `insertDate` options now derive from the current Plate insert-node facade; `DateElement` replaces stale aggregate `TDateElement`, and `@platejs/slate` is a runtime dependency because the emitted package imports the Slate v2 element type.
- tests/oracles: `@platejs/date` `isPointNextToNode` proof no longer passes raw JSX editors through `createSlateEditor({ editor })`; it seeds `value` and `selection`, matching the v2 test fixture boundary.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/excalidraw` `insertExcalidraw` options now derive from the current Plate insert-node facade; stale aggregate `InsertNodesOptions` and the option-bag `as any` spread are gone.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/footnote` `insertFootnote` and the plugin command type now share `InsertFootnoteOptions` derived from the current Plate insert-node facade; stale aggregate `InsertNodesOptions` and the option-bag `as any` cast are gone.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/indent` `setIndent` node-query options now derive from the current Plate `editor.api.nodes` facade instead of stale aggregate `EditorNodesOptions`.
- tests/oracles: `@platejs/indent` `withIndent` normalization proof uses `editor.api.node(path)` instead of aggregate `NodeApi.get(editor, path)`, avoiding a fake v2 helper call on the current Plate editor root.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/layout` column insert/replace/target option types now derive from the current Plate editor facades; stale aggregate `InsertNodesOptions`, `ReplaceNodesOptions`, and `At` imports are gone.
- tests/oracles: `@platejs/layout` normalization specs use `editor.api.node(path)` for live editor lookups, while static child-node traversal stays local and explicit.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/playwright` selection typing now uses Slate v2 `Selection`; the browser adapter reads nodes through the mounted Plate editor API instead of exposing `NodeApi.get`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/selection` block-selection prop options now derive from `PlateEditor['api']['prop']`; inserted-node and selection-rect lookups use the current Plate editor API with Slate v2 static helpers where appropriate, and `@platejs/slate` is a runtime dependency.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/toc` insert options now derive from the current Plate insert-node facade; TOC pure path/element/string helpers use `@platejs/slate`, while live editor lookups use `editor.api.node`.
- tests/oracles: TOC hook mocks now include `api.node`, matching the current editor lookup contract used by the hooks.
- workflow/tooling: migration scanner now supports a `legacy-dependency` quarantine override so a proven package-level legacy runtime boundary does not keep re-entering the package queue as fake work.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/media` lib/react insertion and placeholder transforms no longer import stale aggregate `InsertNodesOptions` / `SetNodesOptions`; current-runtime option aliases derive from `SlateEditor['tf']` or `PlateEditor['tf']`, and option-bag `as any` casts were removed from the touched insert/set transforms.
- tests/oracles: `@platejs/media` `withImageEmbed.spec.tsx` no longer seeds a Plate editor with aggregate `createEditor`; it uses `createSlateEditor({ value, selection })`, matching the post-hard-cut fixture boundary.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/callout` `insertCallout` no longer imports stale aggregate `InsertNodesOptions` or casts insert options through `as any`; its option alias derives from the current Plate `SlateEditor['tf']['insertNodes']` facade until the runtime call site moves to raw Slate v2 APIs.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/link` insert/wrap/unwrap/upsert option aliases no longer import stale aggregate option types; they derive from the current `SlateEditor['tf']` facade, `upsertLink` uses editor-owned leaf lookup, and `BaseLinkPlugin` derives autolink range-before options from `SlateEditor['api']['range']` instead of a fake Slate v2 export or direct legacy import.
- tests/oracles: `@platejs/link` `upsertLink.spec.tsx` no longer wraps hyperscript fixtures in aggregate `createEditor(...)`; fixtures pass parsed children/selection into `createSlateEditor`, which caught and repaired the empty-editor regression in the test setup.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/dnd` no longer imports stale aggregate `EditorNodesOptions` / `ValueOf` or aggregate `Editor` for current Plate editor helpers; block query options derive from `PlateEditor['api']['nodes']`, DnD helper APIs use `PlateEditor`, and hover live-node lookup uses `editor.api.node`.
- docs/examples: static/editor guide snippets in English and Chinese no longer teach `Descendant` from raw `slate` or stale `TElement` / `TText` editor types.
- workflow/tooling: migration scanner now detects stale aggregate option/helper exports beyond `T*` names and supports explicit quarantines through `hit-overrides.json`; `apps/www` upstream Slate comparison imports are quarantined instead of fake-migrated.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `withDeleteForwardList` no longer imports legacy helper/type APIs; it uses `SlateEditor['tf']['deleteForward']`, v2 `PathApi`, editor-owned `api.node`, and direct element child access.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `toggleList` uses Slate v2 `RangeApi` / `PathApi.common` plus editor-owned node lookup for expanded-range common-node detection.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `moveListItemUp` no longer imports legacy helpers; it owns root-path next-list and last-child semantics locally instead of depending on broad legacy `NodeApi` / `PathApi`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `withNormalizeList` no longer imports legacy helpers; list-root child iteration is direct from the current element entry and previous-sibling semantics use the list-owned safe helper.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `normalizeListItem` no longer imports legacy traversal helpers; recursive block cleanup uses typed local child entries and Slate v2 path helpers.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `withInsertFragmentList` now uses Slate v2 detached-node `NodeApi` / `PathApi` and editor-owned live node lookup; it no longer imports `@platejs/slate-legacy`.
- reverted/quarantined packets: `@platejs/list-classic` keeps `deleteMerge` on explicit `@platejs/slate-legacy` imports because it is a full delete/merge runtime algorithm, not a traversal helper.
- code/runtime/API: added `queryNode` to `@platejs/core`; `@platejs/utils` imports Slate primitives from `@platejs/slate` and exports `NodeMap` instead of `TNodeMap`; `@platejs/test-utils` fixture factory uses `@platejs/slate` primitives without legacy deps and keeps direct fixture `.children`/`.selection`; `@platejs/table` runtime/merge/query/transform/spec generic structures use Slate v2 `Element`/`Descendant`/`Range`/`Location`; `@platejs/basic-nodes` blockquote shape uses `Element` from `@platejs/slate`; `@platejs/code-drawing` code drawing shape uses `Element` from `@platejs/slate` and exports `CodeDrawingElement`; `@platejs/excalidraw` drawing shape uses `Element` from `@platejs/slate` and exports `ExcalidrawElement`; `@platejs/find-replace` search ranges use `Range` from `@platejs/slate`; `@platejs/math` markdown rule ranges use `Range` from `@platejs/slate`; `@platejs/combobox` trigger input nodes use `Element` from `@platejs/slate`; `@platejs/comment` comment guards no longer depend on legacy `TNode`; `@platejs/layout` column transforms use column-specific element types instead of generic legacy primitives; `@platejs/media` upload history uses `TMediaElement` instead of generic legacy `TElement`; `@platejs/playwright` harness location/path types use `@platejs/slate` and returned node handles are intentionally `unknown`; `@platejs/caption` uses caption-specific element types and Slate v2 `Range`; `@platejs/floating` geometry helpers use Slate v2 `Location`/`Range`; `@platejs/toc` insertion/query helpers use Slate v2 `Element`; `@platejs/cursor` overlay state uses Slate v2 `Range`; `@platejs/link` transforms/rules use Slate v2 `Text`/`Range`; `@platejs/diff` structural diff helpers use Slate v2 `Element`/`Text`/`Descendant` while editor operations stay Plate-owned; `@platejs/markdown` serializer/deserializer structural types use Slate v2 `Element`/`Text`/`Descendant`; `@platejs/footnote` APIs/registry/transforms use `FootnoteElement` plus Slate v2 structural types while editor APIs stay Plate-owned; `@platejs/dnd` drag/drop element contracts use Slate v2 `Element`; `@platejs/code-block` code-line/code-block structural helpers use Slate v2 `Element`/`Location`; `@platejs/suggestion` transforms/queries use Slate v2 structural primitives while suggestion-specific data shapes and editor APIs stay Plate-owned; `@platejs/selection` block-selection and cursor-overlay helpers use Slate v2 `Element`/`Text`/`Range`, and `selectBlocks` takes the path target it actually supports; `@platejs/ai` markdown/streaming/copilot/suggestion helpers use Slate v2 `Element`/`Text`/`Descendant`/`Range`/`Location` while editor, table, and suggestion-specific APIs stay Plate-owned; `@platejs/list` list hooks/transforms/queries/normalizers use Slate v2 `Element`/`Descendant`/`Location` while list-specific generics stay Plate-owned; `@platejs/list-classic` classic list transforms/queries/normalizers/paste-delete plugins use Slate v2 `Element`/`Text`/`Descendant`/`Range`/`Location`, and todo items expose `TodoListItemElement`; `@platejs/core` primitive render/static/node-data/parser/html helper types, render components, selected hooks, structural helpers, and HTML deserializer hyperscript helpers import owned `@platejs/slate*` packages; `platejs` aggregate resolves `queryNode` to core.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` current-runtime tx bridge now supports `tx.nodes.insert`; `@platejs/selection` duplicate selected-block command no longer calls legacy `duplicateNodes`, performs document insertion through tx, and leaves selected-id plugin state outside tx.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `SlateEditor` / React `PlateEditor` now expose typed Slate v2 `editor.update`; the current-runtime bridge supports `tx.nodes.remove`; `@platejs/selection` insert/remove/set/indent/text block-selection document commands use inferred tx and v2 set-node option types.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` current-runtime tx bridge supports `tx.selection.set` / `tx.selection.clear`; `@platejs/selection` `selectBlockSelectionNodes` uses inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx.selection.set(...))` and clears block-selection plugin state outside tx.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` current-runtime tx bridge supports `tx.selection.collapse`; `@platejs/ai` `insertAINodes`, `removeAINodes`, and `removeAIMarks` use inferred `editor.update((tx) => ...)`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` current-runtime tx bridge supports `tx.value.replace`; `SlateExtensionPlugin` `setValue` uses inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx.value.replace(...))` instead of direct legacy `replaceNodes`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` exposes `PluginTx<K, Group>` and generic `editor.update<TTx>()`; tx-backed facades in `@platejs/basic-nodes`, `@platejs/basic-styles`, `@platejs/code-block`, `@platejs/comment`, and `@platejs/list-classic` now use typed plugin transaction groups instead of `(editor as any).update((tx: any) => ...)`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` plugin config/method types now carry an inferred `tx` slot through `extendTx`, Slate plugin contexts expose that tx group inside `editor.update((tx) => ...)`, and `toPlatePlugin` preserves tx metadata instead of erasing it.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` typed Slate/Plate editors and the v2 `PlateRuntimeEditor` now carry installed plugin tx groups into `editor.update`, so runtime/plugin proof can use inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx.plugin.command())` instead of explicit `PluginTx` generics or update casts.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` input-rule insert-text context now owns `InsertTextOptions` from Slate v2 `TextInsertTextOptions` plus Plate's `marks` flag; the only mismatch with the current legacy insert-text transform is isolated in `InputRulesPlugin` as a named bridge cast.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` specs no longer import Plate editor factory/types from aggregate `platejs` or create legacy fixture editors in the targeted list-query/transform specs; Plate test helpers come from `@platejs/core`.
- code/runtime/API: `platejs` aggregate explicitly exports Plate core `createSlateEditor` while continuing to export Slate primitives; raw Slate users should import from `@platejs/slate`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `TSlateEditor` now extends `SlateEditor` directly, preserving assignability into current-runtime package algorithms while retaining typed plugin tx inference.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` runtime/source imports now name direct owners: Plate editor/plugin helpers from `@platejs/core`, Slate v2 structures from `@platejs/slate`, constants from `@platejs/utils`, and utility bind/type helpers from `@udecode/utils`; aggregate `platejs` remains only in the hook spec that intentionally mocks the public aggregate.
- package/DX: `@platejs/list-classic` now declares the direct runtime dependencies it imports: `@platejs/core`, `@platejs/slate`, `@platejs/utils`, and `@udecode/utils`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` low-risk query/delete-fragment helpers now use Slate v2 structural/static APIs where safe: `hasListChild` uses `ElementApi`, `isAcrossListItems` uses v2 `RangeApi.isCollapsed`, and touched files keep only runtime-bound legacy `PathApi` / `deleteMerge`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` pure path helpers in `getHighestEmptyList`, `insertListItem`, and `insertTodoListItem` now use Slate v2 `PathApi`; more semantic helpers like `PathApi.previous` stay untouched until covered by source-specific proof.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` tab/unhang list behavior now uses Slate v2 `RangeApi.isBackward` in `withList`; focused `withList` and full package proof stay green.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` list-entry query helpers now use Slate v2 `RangeApi` and editor-owned `api.node` path validation; `getListItemEntry` and `getTodoListItemEntry` no longer import legacy helpers.
- tests/oracles: `@platejs/list-classic` `normalizeListItem.spec` now uses editor-owned `api.node` fixture lookup instead of legacy `NodeApi.get`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `unwrapList` common-node fallback now uses v2 `PathApi.common` plus current editor `api.node`; its spec no longer spies on legacy internals.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` `moveListItems` now uses Slate v2 path/location types and pure `PathApi` helpers; no legacy option/path imports remain there.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` move-to-list helpers now compute append positions from destination `children.length` instead of legacy `NodeApi.lastChild` / `PathApi.next`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` sibling-move helper now uses v2 `PathApi`, editor-owned `api.node`, and direct list-type checks instead of legacy `NodeApi` / `match`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` now owns `getPreviousSiblingPath` for safe previous-sibling semantics; `moveListItemDown` and `normalizeNestedList` no longer import legacy helpers.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/list-classic` delete paths now keep only legacy `deleteMerge`; ordinary path helpers moved to Slate v2/local list helpers.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/basic-nodes` mark/heading/blockquote tx-backed facades now use inferred `editor.update((tx) => tx[plugin.key].toggle())` with no `PluginTx` generic scaffolding.
- tests/oracles: `createSlatePlugin.spec.ts` covers inferred tx groups in later plugin extension contexts; `BaseBlockquotePlugin.spec.ts` explicitly uses legacy `NodeApi` because it exercises the current legacy Plate runtime editor.
- workflow slowdown: the first `@platejs/basic-nodes` package test failure was caused by running build/test/lint in parallel while `dist` was being rewritten; package tests need to run after build/lint when package `dist` can change.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` current-runtime `editor.update` migration scaffold is isolated in `legacyRuntimeUpdateBridge.ts`; `withSlate` now only installs the named bridge, and focused proof covers inferred update callbacks plus the explicit unsupported `afterCommit` boundary.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` current-runtime `withSlate` now installs typed plugin option mutators through `SlateEditor['setOption']` / `SlateEditor['setOptions']` instead of local `any` parameter signatures; symbol option keys are stringified explicitly in debug output.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` Plate store/provider typing now uses a minimal `PlateStoreEditor` contract and a generic `PlateStoreProviderProps`, so `PlateInner<E>` is cast-free and `Plate.tsx` no longer needs `props as any` or `props as PlateProps`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` public `Plate` now accepts the minimal `PlateRootEditor` contract instead of full legacy `PlateEditor`; focused proof mounts `createPlateRuntimeEditor` under `Plate` with `PlateRuntimeContent`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `useEditorRef` and `useEditorState` now accept generic `PlateStoreEditor` implementations, so `PlateRuntimeEditor<Value>` can be read from the public Plate store hooks with inferred `editor.update((tx) => ...)` instead of a legacy `PlateEditor` cast.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` public `PlateContent` now detects branded v2 runtime editors and routes them to `PlateRuntimeContent` plus `PlateContentStateEffect`, while legacy editor content stays on the old `PlateSlate` / legacy `Editable` path.
- code/runtime/API: `platejs` aggregate exports now hard-cut from `@platejs/slate-legacy` to `@platejs/slate`; Slate v2 `BaseEditor` is explicitly selected to resolve the aggregate star-export conflict with `@platejs/core`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `PlateRuntimeEditor` now infers installed plugin tx groups from `createPlateRuntimeEditor({ plugins })`, so the future v2 runtime scaffold proves plugin tx groups with plain `editor.update((tx) => tx.txPlugin.replace())`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `PlateRuntimePlugin` now owns `useHooks` metadata directly, so the v2 runtime scaffold no longer casts plugin metadata just to fill `pluginCache.useHooks`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` v2 runtime scaffold now types installed plugins and plugin-list metadata as `PlateRuntimePlugin` instead of `unknown`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` v2 runtime scaffold/spec no longer contain local `any` casts or `PlateRuntimeEditor<any, any>` aliases; generic helpers preserve the runtime editor type, while unresolved plugin metadata editor access is explicitly `unknown`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` now has an internal `PlateRuntimeSlate` v2 provider adapter beside `createPlateRuntimeEditor`; it wraps `@platejs/slate-react` `<Slate>`, applies Plate runtime `aboveSlate` wrappers, defaults read-only from runtime editor DOM state, and does not use the legacy `initialValue` prop.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` now has an internal `PlateRuntimeEditable` v2 content adapter beside `PlateRuntimeSlate`; it wraps `@platejs/slate-react` `<Editable>`, applies Plate runtime `beforeEditable`, `aboveEditable`, and `afterEditable` wrappers, supports `renderEditable`, runs plugin `useHooks` under the v2 provider and wrapped editable branch, and does not replace old `PlateContent` store/effect/hotkey/controller behavior yet.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` now has an internal `PlateRuntimeContent` v2 content entrypoint that composes `PlateRuntimeSlate` and `PlateRuntimeEditable`, forwards Slate callbacks and editable props, and preserves value/extension generic typing across provider and editable layers.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `PlateContent` effect behavior is isolated into internal `PlateContentEffects` and `PlateContentStateEffect`; render-local methods/hotkeys/ref/controller effects stay beside the editable, state/callback/autofocus sync stays directly under `PlateSlate`, and the current legacy `Editable` prop mismatch is quarantined behind a named `unknown` bridge instead of `as any`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` DOM plugin now owns its public `ScrollIntoViewOptions` type from `scroll-into-view-if-needed` directly instead of importing it through `@platejs/slate-legacy`; core declares the dependency because its public DOM plugin options reference that type.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` slate-extension `liftBlock` / `insertExitBreak` now use a local object-or-function match helper instead of legacy `EditorAboveOptions` / `combineMatchOptions`; `insertExitBreak` still intentionally keeps legacy `PathApi.next` until path helper edge semantics are migrated deliberately.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` slate-extension `resetBlock` now uses v2 `NodeApi.extractProps` with an explicit element-prop narrowing instead of legacy `NodeApi`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` break-rules `splitReset` path calculation now uses v2 `PathApi.next`; behavior is covered by the full `withBreakRules` focused spec.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` slate-extension `insertExitBreak` now uses v2 `PathApi.next`; focused exit-break/lift specs cover the migration.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` affinity mark-boundary query now imports `IS_FIREFOX` from `@platejs/slate-dom` and uses v2 `NodeApi.extractProps`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` affinity static helpers now use v2 `ElementApi`, `TextApi`, and `NodeApi.extractProps/string`; legacy `NodeApi.get` remains only where the current Plate editor root is still legacy-shaped.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` navigation feedback now resolves flash targets through `editor.api.node(path)` instead of importing legacy `NodeApi.get`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `isType` utility proof now uses `createSlateEditor({ value })` instead of importing legacy `createEditor` and JSX hyperscript fixtures.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `EditableProps` imports `DOMRange` from `@platejs/slate-dom`, and `scrollSelectionIntoView` now receives Plate `SlateEditor` instead of legacy `Editor`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `pipeOnChange` proof no longer imports legacy `createEditor`; it relies on `createPlateEditor` as the package-owned construction API.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` chunking config imports structural `Ancestor` from `@platejs/slate`; the default query keeps `LegacyNodeApi.isEditor` explicitly because it tests the current legacy editor runtime, and `SlateEditor` now declares the optional plugin-installed `getChunkSize` method.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` React plugin/fallback utility files no longer import `LegacyEditorMethods`; local current-runtime bridge types derive root `insertData` / `apply` from the Plate transform surface instead of widening `SlateEditor` with legacy root methods.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `init` uses Slate v2 `Selection` / `Value` types; direct lifecycle assignment remains under the current legacy runtime because the tx rewrite attempt changed startup operations.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` React provider support types in `useSlateProps`, `useNodePath`, Plate stores, element stores, Plate slow tests, and `createPlateTestEditor` now use `@platejs/slate` structural types instead of `@platejs/slate-legacy`; `useNodePath` takes `Descendant`, not broad v2 `Node`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` React editor entrypoints use Slate v2 `Value` generics in `withPlate`, `usePlateEditor`, and `usePlateViewEditor`; the legacy `Editor/createEditor` import remains explicit in `withPlate` as the runtime constructor boundary.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `pipeOnChange` and TPlateEditor specs now use Slate v2 `Value`; render-leaf hard-affinity utilities use editor-owned `api.node` for live text lookup instead of legacy `NodeApi.get`.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` `BasePlugin`, `SlatePlugin`, `PlatePlugin`, static renderer, `EditableProps.decorate`, and `pipeDecorate` now use Slate v2 structural vocabulary (`Element`, `Text`, `Range`, operation/value types); legacy remains only for current Plate runtime API/transform contracts, DOM editor callback, and decoration equality helpers.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` editor type roots now use Slate v2 `Value`, `Range`, and `Selection` in `SlateEditor`, `PlateEditor`, and `withSlate`; legacy `Operation`, `EditorBase`, `EditorApi`, `EditorTransforms`, and `createEditor` stay explicit runtime-bound contracts.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` static editor factory now uses Slate v2 `Value` while keeping legacy `Editor/createEditor` as the explicit constructor boundary.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` affinity tuple/plugin/query types now use Slate v2 `Element` / `Text` / `Path` / `NodeEntry`; `getEdgeNodes` uses Slate v2 `ElementApi` / `PathApi` and editor-owned parent/node lookup, while deeper affinity runtime helpers still keep explicit legacy imports where current editor-root behavior is not migrated.
- code/runtime/API: `@platejs/core` Slate extension handler/config/node/text types now use Slate v2 `Descendant`, `Element`, `Text`, `NodeOperation`, and `TextOperation`; legacy operation/node/path helper imports remain runtime-bound.

- tests: `@platejs/link` package proof covers paste/input autolink, `upsertLink`, floating-link triggers, URL validation, unwrap/wrap behavior, and declaration build after the production type cleanup.
- changesets: none by explicit user instruction.
- skills/workflow: scanner now avoids Slate-substrate generic false positives by tying stale `T*` hits to legacy/bare Slate sources or docs text.
- skills/workflow: added command-surface inventory tooling and ledgers for plugin API/transform/editor-mutation rows; latest scan found 312 rows across 30 owners, now split by raw transform debt, core command facades, mixed transform facades, runtime-backed rows, deferred runtime owners, spec fixtures, and accepted tx-backed facades; `packages/core` has 0 raw transform rows, 0 legacy batch transform rows, 5 runtime-backed transform rows, and 179 test fixture rows.
- skills/workflow: widened command-surface scanner tx-backed-facade lookback so large inline `extendTx` groups are not misclassified as raw transform debt.
- skills/workflow: added command-surface scanner `legacy-batch-transform-decision` so commands with `withoutSaving(setNodesBatch(...))` route to runtime/batch architecture instead of fake tx wrapping.
- skills/workflow: added command-surface scanner `core-command-facade-decision` so package facades over core editor transforms route to the core runtime transform owner.
- skills/workflow: scanner row granularity is still plugin-block-level for `extendTransforms`; use source-backed mixed-facade classifications for blocks that intentionally combine tx-backed commands with state/history/focus/runtime commands instead of treating them as simple tx candidates.
- skills/workflow: package transform code should not use `(editor as any).update((tx: any) => ...)`; add/repair the typed editor update surface in core before migrating more tx commands.
- reverted/quarantined packets: reverted bad `@platejs/core -> @platejs/callout` devDependency attempt; reverted/quarantined affinity `NodeApi`, `PlateStatic`, and `withChunking` migrations because they still depend on legacy editor/decorate/plugin contracts.

Needs your attention:
1. `packages/slate-legacy` is still intentional scaffold. Do not delete it
   until the full Plate runtime/default-route migration proves no current
   editor/runtime contract depends on it.
2. Deferred runtime owners are explicit, not forgotten: `packages/ai`,
   `packages/list-classic`, `packages/media`, `packages/selection`,
   `packages/suggestion`, and `packages/table`. Each needs its own behavior
   packet before claiming Slate v2 runtime parity.
3. `apps/www` playground proof is green through the current Plate proof adapter
   and `@platejs/browser/playwright`. That proves the current playground route,
   not the future default Slate v2 Plate runtime for every plugin.
4. Public package-specific `T*` names still exist where they are shared Plate
   public API (`@platejs/utils` table/math shapes, etc.). Those belong to a
   later Plate v2 API cleanup lane, not this package-by-package migration.
5. `AnyPluginConfig` still intentionally has broad carrier fields. The safe
   type recovery is installed plugin tx inference plus the isolated
   `legacyRuntimeUpdateBridge.ts`; fully strict plugin carrier typing needs a
   deliberate core generic redesign.

Workflow slowdowns:
| Step / command | Owner | Elapsed / estimate | Why slow | Evidence | Repair decision |
|----------------|-------|--------------------|----------|----------|-----------------|
| CSV/Markdown API proof boundary | core/csv/markdown | short | first package proof used raw Slate `editor.getApi(PlatePlugin)`, then serial proof failed when CSV hit v2 runtime `getType` missing-plugin throw; later a parallel build/test rerun read half-rewritten aggregate dist | failures: `Editor extension "undefined" is not installed`, `[Plate] Plugin "table" is not installed`, and `Cannot find module '@platejs/core' from packages/plate/dist/index.js` during a build/test overlap | use `editor.getPluginApi<T>(plugin)` for Plate plugin APIs, make runtime `getType` fallback to key without weakening `getPlugin`, and keep package tests that read built dist serial with builds |
| filtered package test still exposed package-wide failures | utils | short | `pnpm --filter @platejs/utils test -- src/lib/plugins/ExitBreakPlugin.spec.ts` ran the package lane and exposed stale single-block hyperscript fixtures, not just the named spec | ExitBreak v2 proof passed, but `SingleBlockPlugin` / `SingleLinePlugin` failed because `createEditor(<editor>...)` fixtures no longer preserved `.children` under the current fixture shape | treat package test failures as real package-owner signal; repair stale oracles before counting the packet green |
| helper type guard cannot be passed directly to `Array.filter` | caption | short | Slate v2 `NodeApi.isNode(value, options?)` has an optional second parameter, which collides with `filter`'s numeric index argument when passed directly | first caption typecheck failed on `caption.filter(NodeApi.isNode)` despite runtime tests passing | use named local type guards around Slate v2 helpers when helper signatures have extra options parameters |
| broad package mocks hide exact module contracts | emoji | short | broad `../../lib`, `../utils`, and one-function `platejs/react` mocks masked direct imports and polluted singleton state once production code moved to direct owners | `@platejs/emoji` first failed on missing `usePluginOption`, then on a fake `EmojiFloatingIndexSearch` library, then on missed `insertEmoji` direct import after barrel cleanup | preserve real public package mocks with spreads, mock exact direct modules, and reset singleton state after specs that bind singleton instances |
| tx type owner confusion | list-classic | short | `EditorUpdateTransaction` is a Slate v2 public transaction type, but the first package cleanup imported it from `@platejs/core` | `pnpm turbo typecheck --filter=./packages/list-classic` failed on missing `EditorUpdateTransaction` export and an implicit node parameter | import transaction types from `@platejs/slate`, keep package facades inferred through `editor.update`, and add public-path tx inference specs |
| fake partial override context | footnote | short | `withTriggerCombobox` is typed as a reusable `overrideEditor` function and expects the full override context, not a hand-built object containing only `insertText` | first footnote typecheck rejected `tf: { insertText }` as missing the rest of the transform surface | pass the real override context to reusable override helpers; destructure the transforms needed by local wrapper code after that |
| table focused proof widened to package run | table | short | the table package test script does not behave like a tiny single-spec proof when invoked through the package filter, and an earlier parallel proof overlapped with dist reads | full `@platejs/table` package test passed serially; earlier parallel run produced stale `@udecode/react-hotkeys` dist/module noise before serial proof passed | keep table package proof serial and treat package-wide fallout as owner signal; do not diagnose parallel stale-dist failures as table logic |
| over-tight Slate element guard | toggle | short | the first toggle cleanup replaced a loose index-record contract with `ElementApi.isElement`, but toggle index helpers intentionally accept shallow records in tests and state derivation | `@platejs/toggle` first package test failed: `getLastEntryEnclosedInToggle(editor, 't1')` returned `undefined` for shallow `{ id, indent, type }` records | type the real package-local contract as an indexable record with string `id`; do not force full Slate element shape unless the owner truly needs `children` |
| inferred hook return not declaration-portable | link | short | removing `: any` from exported floating-link hooks passed source typecheck but made package build emit inferred return types that referenced pnpm-internal `csstype` symbols | first `@platejs/link build` failed with TS2883 on `useFloatingLinkEdit` inferred return type needing `.pnpm/csstype...` names | exported hooks need explicit portable return types when they return React style/DOM prop objects; source inference alone is not enough for public package DX |
| InputRules metadata was only half-resolved | core | short | `createPlateRuntimeEditor` stored per-plugin `rules` arrays but left executable insertBreak/insertData/insertText buckets empty, so adding only transform wrappers would have produced no-op runtime rules | source audit showed `createRuntimeInputRulesMeta` never filled `meta.inputRules.insertText.byTrigger`, `insertBreak`, or `insertData`; the new test would fail without bucket population | port the existing resolver semantics into the v2 runtime metadata builder before routing transforms |
| Length v2 deletion API mismatch | core | short | the legacy clamp used `editor.tf.delete({ distance, reverse })`, but v2 directed deletion is not `deleteBackward({ distance })` | first typecheck rejected the naive `deleteBackward({ distance })` rewrite even though the behavior test had passed | use `tx.text.delete({ distance, reverse: true, unit: 'character' })`, the v2 API that owns distance |
| Affinity exact mark state gap | slate/core | medium | Affinity needs to distinguish `{}` from `null` insertion marks; `tx.marks.add/remove/toggle` could not express that exactly | the first substrate test showed public `state.marks.get()` resolves inherited marks, so raw null is the wrong proof target | add public `tx.marks.set(marks)` and prove inserted document shape for explicit marks, empty marks, and inherited marks |

| SlateExtension callback pipeline silently skipped primary-root reads | core | short | v2 operation middleware receives internal `root: "main"` for primary-root operations, while public `state.value.root("main")` intentionally throws; the first helper caught that throw and returned `undefined`, so callbacks never fired | focused runtime tests failed because configured `onNodeChange` / `onTextChange` were not called; direct commit logging showed real `set_node` / `insert_text` operations; direct middleware invocation showed the callback code worked when root was absent | normalize internal `main` to an omitted root only inside the runtime read helper; keep public API docs free of `main` |

| content adapter generic mismatch | core/react-runtime | short | first `PlateRuntimeContent` implementation composed the right runtime pieces but passed `children` through a prop shape that React lint rejects and let `PlateRuntimeEditable` default back to a non-extension-specific editor type | first `pnpm turbo typecheck --filter=./packages/core` failed on missing children / editor api extension mismatch; first lint failed on `noChildrenProp`; final typecheck and lint passed after threading value/extension generics through editable props and using React children args | preserve editor value/extension generics across every runtime adapter layer; never fix this with `any` |
| PlateContent effect extraction ordering | core/react-components | short | first extraction moved state sync into the editable wrapper subtree and left the old `EditorStateEffect` call in place, so the refactor was not behavior-neutral | `PlateContent.spec.tsx` and the package wrapper failed with `ReferenceError: EditorStateEffect is not defined`; final proof passed after splitting render-local effects from state sync and preserving the old order | extract behavior by contract and order, not just by grouping nearby hooks |
| list-classic v2 helper mix | list-classic | medium | after the aggregate hard cut, list algorithms mixed Slate v2 helper imports with current legacy editor fixtures | full list-classic test initially failed broad rows until `match`, `deleteMerge`, `NodeApi`, `PathApi`, and `RangeApi` were made explicit `@platejs/slate-legacy` imports | keep current-runtime list algorithms honest until the real list tx/runtime owner rewrites them |
| hidden legacy scaffold dependencies | code-block/list-classic | short | package builds depended on bundled current-runtime code that still imports upstream `slate` / `slate-dom` | list-classic build warned until `@platejs/slate-legacy`, `slate`, and `slate-dom` were declared in package manifests and `pnpm install` refreshed the lockfile | declare temporary scaffold deps explicitly; do not hide them behind aggregate exports |
| code-block fixture used v2 editor creation for legacy paste behavior | code-block | short | code-block paste specs still exercised legacy Slate hyperscript/current-runtime behavior but imported `createEditor` from the aggregate after the hard cut | three paste rows failed until the spec imported fixture `createEditor` / `Descendant` from `@platejs/slate-legacy` | use v2 fixtures only when the behavior target is the v2 runtime |
| code-block generic element inference | code-block | short | `getCodeLineEntry` used `ElementOf<SlateEditor>`, which resolves to `never` for the current Plate editor type and hid behind legacy helper usage until runtime helpers were removed | first code-block typecheck failed with `Property 'children' does not exist on type 'never'`; simplifying the helper to return concrete `NodeEntry<Element>` made the real owner type explicit | prefer concrete package element-entry shapes over fake editor-wide generics when the editor type cannot infer the value schema |
| list-classic aggregate editor factory ambiguity | list-classic/plate/core | short | after the aggregate hard cut, specs importing `createSlateEditor` from `platejs` got the wrong v2-shaped editor surface and `TSlateEditor` was no longer assignable to `SlateEditor` because the prior editor type shape lost base members | list-classic typecheck failed broadly with `editor.getType` unknown and missing `id` / `history` / `marks` / `operations` / `selection`; direct package tests still passed once the fixture boundary was corrected | specs import Plate editor helpers from `@platejs/core`; aggregate explicitly exports Plate core `createSlateEditor`; core `TSlateEditor` extends `SlateEditor` directly |
| greedy import-owner codemod guard | list-classic/tooling | tiny | first mechanical import rewrite matched across unrelated imports because the parser used a broad multi-line pattern | unknown-symbol guard aborted before writes; the stricter import pattern rewrote 46 files and proof stayed green | keep mechanical rewrites guarded by explicit unknown-symbol failure; do not hand-wave broad codemods in package migrations |
| visible migration hit count rose after owner split | migration tooling/list-classic | tiny | replacing aggregate `platejs` imports with direct `@platejs/slate` owner imports increases scanner visibility even though legacy debt did not grow | owner inventory still shows list-classic at 27 legacy hits and package proof green; total visible hits rose to 3045 | read owner rows, not just raw total hits, after import-owner cleanup packets |

Findings:
- `packages/utils` was a good first full package migration: it can consume Slate v2 primitives without waiting on the Plate runtime rewrite.
- `packages/table` had only test-surface direct legacy usage; package behavior stayed green.
- `packages/test-utils` can migrate without `@platejs/slate-legacy`, but it must keep a local Plate fixture factory because Plate specs intentionally read direct fixture fields.

Decisions and tradeoffs:
- Keep structural Plate helpers like `queryNode` in `@platejs/core`, not in Slate substrate.
- Delete copied fixture internals only when the replacement preserves fixture semantics; here a local fixture owner is justified.
- Do not create changesets in this lane.

Review fixes:
- Core test graph repaired by removing product-plugin dependency from core specs.

Loop 258 addendum:
- Packet: `caption-runtime-route`.
- Owner: `packages/core` runtime scaffold plus `packages/caption` caption override row.
- Why: `BaseCaptionPlugin` was a one-row editor-runtime owner. Current Plate wraps `apply` and `moveLine` to focus caption textareas after ArrowUp selection movement or down-line movement into an allowed captioned element. The v2 runtime needed the same behavior through operation middleware and transform routing, not a package-local fake tx facade.
- Changed list: `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now consumes caption override metadata as `runtimeCaption`, reconstructs the next collapsed selection from `set_selection` operations, finds allowed caption targets through Slate v2 state queries, schedules `focusEndPath` when ArrowUp lands on a captioned node with text, and wraps `moveLine({ reverse: false })` to focus the caption for the active allowed block. - Tests/oracles: focused runtime proof covers dynamic selectability, open Enter, closed Enter, Backspace across a hidden child, and Delete across a hidden child. The Backspace oracle deliberately preserves hidden child content on the v2 route; the current legacy path can drop the only hidden child in one edge case while retaining hidden children in the multi-child case, and the content-preserving v2 behavior is the better invariant.
- Proof: `pnpm turbo typecheck --filter=./packages/core --filter=./packages/toggle` passed; `pnpm --filter @platejs/toggle test -- ToggleRuntimePlugin.spec.ts withToggle.spec.tsx BaseTogglePlugin.spec.ts someToggle.spec.ts` passed 16 tests / 33 assertions; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core test -- src/react/editor/createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` passed 934 tests / 2251 assertions with existing multiple-core-instance warnings only; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core lint:fix && pnpm --filter @platejs/toggle lint:fix` passed; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core build && pnpm --filter @platejs/toggle build` passed; command-surface scanner passed with 312 rows / 30 owners and now marks both toggle rows runtime-backed; stale migration scanner passed with 5384 files / 1 stale owner / 2623 hits / 0 missing current Slate deps; focused bad-update audit over core runtime, toggle source, and scanner returned no `(editor as any).update`, `update((tx: any)`, `tx: any`, or `editor as any` hits.
- Keep/revert/quarantine: keep. The current-runtime `withToggle` override remains in the package source until Plate fully swaps runtime, but the v2 runtime route is explicit and package-proven. Existing `any` casts remain in older toggle test fixtures and mocks; they are not runtime update casts or production command code.
- Workflow slowdown: the first Backspace oracle copied a single-child legacy outcome that deletes hidden content. A second legacy sample showed the multi-child path keeps hidden content. The v2 route keeps hidden content and documents that as the chosen invariant rather than preserving a destructive edge.
- Needs review: medium. Taste-sensitive point: v2 intentionally does not port the destructive single-hidden-child Backspace edge. This is a Plate behavior break, but it is a good one: closed toggle content should not vanish just because a visible block behind it is merged.
- Next owner: choose another small runtime row such as `packages/code-block` if we want a contained block algorithm, or defer to a broader selection/media/table lane only after an explicit owner split.

- Workflow slowdown: package tests can execute stale built `@platejs/core` / aggregate `platejs` output; rebuild core after runtime source changes before trusting package-test failures. The first fragment oracle only checked value shape and would have missed a real cursor bug; behavior packets need selection assertions when the user-visible operation moves the caret.
- Needs review: low. The only taste-sensitive bit is that fragment insertion may be two updates when additional lines exist: one structural insertion update plus one final selection update. If history grouping later treats this as two undo steps, fold it under an explicit history-group proof.
- Next owner: continue code-block with `insertData` paste/data behavior, or move to another contained runtime owner if we want to avoid staying in one broad package.

Loop 278 addendum:
- Packet: `code-block-runtime-lowlight-apply-redecorate-slice`.
- Owner: `packages/slate`, `packages/core`, `packages/code-block`, and this plan.
- Why: loop 277 left the final `withCodeBlock` behavior open: lowlight decoration cache invalidation and editor `redecorate()` on code-block language changes. The first v2 route surfaced a deeper Slate v2 API-capability bug: duplicate callable capabilities under one API name resolved to `{}` through object merging, so `editor.api.redecorate` could become non-callable when the default no-op and mounted override both existed.
- Changed list: `packages/slate/src/create-editor.ts` now resolves duplicate API capabilities by merging only object capability groups and using latest-wins for callable/scalar capabilities. `packages/slate/test/extension-methods-contract.ts` proves object groups still merge and callable shared API names restore the previous callable after cleanup. `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now detects code-block `set_node` language changes in the Slate v2 runtime, calls a callable `editor.api.redecorate` only when present, and leaves unrelated property changes alone. `BaseCodeBlockPlugin` now recomputes lowlight decorations when the cached code-block language differs from the current `lang` / `defaultLanguage`. `setCodeBlockToDecorations` records the effective language per code block and removes old local `any` casts with `unknown`-based Lowlight node narrowing. `CodeBlockRuntimePlugin.spec.ts` proves lowlight language changes redecorate in the v2 runtime and unrelated code-block property changes do not.
- Tests/oracles: added Slate API-capability contract tests for object merge vs callable latest-wins; added code-block v2 runtime redecorate/no-op proof; retained current-runtime `withCodeBlock` apply/redecorate tests and the full code-block runtime behavior suite.

Loop 289 addendum:

- Owner: `packages/core`, migration tooling, and this plan.
- Why: `NodeIdPlugin.normalize` was the last core
  `legacy-batch-transform-decision` row. The behavior is a maintenance batch

  right update metadata to skip history.
- Changed list: `createPlateRuntimeEditor.ts` now installs a runtime
  `nodeId.normalize()` transform for `NodeIdPlugin`, collects missing-id updates
  with text/inline/block filtering, writes through inferred
  `editor.update((tx) => tx.nodes.set(...))`, and passes
  `{ metadata: { history: { mode: 'skip' } }, skipNormalize: true }`.
  `createPlateRuntimeEditor.spec.ts` proves the transform assigns ids to nested
  block elements, leaves text nodes untouched, and does not create undo history.
  `scan-plate-command-surface.mjs` now classifies the NodeId normalize row as a
  runtime-backed transform facade, and regenerated command-surface artifacts
  show zero legacy batch transform rows.

  `useNavigationHighlight` calling Slate v2 `useElementPath`, which requires
  the Slate v2 `<Slate>` selector context. The playground is still current
  Plate runtime, so navigation feedback must not read Slate v2 element-path
  context on that branch.
- Changed list: `packages/core/src/react/plugins/navigation-feedback/useNavigationHighlight.ts`
  now reads the existing Plate element context path through `useElementContext`
  and keeps explicit node/path resolution through `editor.api.findPath`; this
  removes the cross-provider Slate v2 hook dependency from current Plate
  rendering. `command-surface-ledger.tsv`, `command-surface-summary.md`,
  `hit-ledger.tsv`, `owner-inventory.tsv`, and `summary.md` were refreshed by
  the migration scanners. This plan records the packet.
- Tests/oracles: the focused React navigation-feedback spec proves current
  Plate highlighting still updates attributes without a selection change; the
  app browser proof proves the playground route renders, exposes the Slate
  browser handle adapter, edits text, and undo/redo works through the harness.
- Proof: initial `pnpm --filter www test:slate-browser:chromium
  tests/slate-browser/playground.spec.ts` failed with
  `useEditorSelector` outside Slate v2 `<Slate>`; after the fix, `bun test
  packages/core/src/react/plugins/navigation-feedback/NavigationFeedbackPlugin.spec.tsx
  packages/core/src/lib/plugins/navigation-feedback/NavigationFeedbackPlugin.spec.ts`
  passed 9 tests / 29 assertions; `pnpm turbo typecheck
  --filter=./packages/core` passed; `pnpm --filter www
  test:slate-browser:chromium tests/slate-browser/playground.spec.ts` passed 1
  Chromium playground edit test; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core lint:fix` passed
  with no fixes; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core build` passed; `pnpm --filter
  www typecheck` passed; migration scanner passed with 5391 files / 1 owner /
  2636 hits / 0 missing direct current Slate deps; command-surface scanner
  passed with 313 rows / 30 owners; `node
  .agents/skills/autogoal/scripts/check-complete.mjs
  docs/plans/2026-06-20-plate-package-slate-v2-migration.md` correctly failed
  because the broad migration completion gates remain open.
- Keep/revert/quarantine: keep. This is the correct current-runtime boundary:
  Plate React render hooks may read Plate element context while the route is on
  legacy `PlateContent`; Slate v2 selector hooks stay inside Slate v2 runtime
  rendering.
- Deferred-with-owner: default Plate runtime routing is still the hard core
  checkpoint; the playground proof works through the current Plate proof
  adapter, not a claim that every Plate plugin is on the v2 runtime path.
- Workflow slowdown: the first proof failure was useful and should not be
  weakened. The app browser row is the right guard for accidental Slate v2 hook
  leakage into current Plate branches.
- Needs review: low. The only taste-sensitive point is preserving current
  Plate context compatibility while the full runtime swap remains deferred.
- Next owner: core runtime/helper-boundary retirement checkpoint or one
  explicitly deferred runtime package owner from the command-surface ledger.

Loop 334 addendum:
- Packet: `core-current-runtime-private-bridge`.
- Owner: `packages/core` current Plate runtime constructor/type/history/plugin
  resolution boundary.
- Why: user reopened foundation migration with a stricter rule: remove direct
  `@platejs/slate-legacy` imports, keep packages green, and allow only
  temporary private bridges. The remaining core imports were real current
  runtime contracts, not safe Slate v2 helper swaps.
- Changed list: added
  `packages/core/src/internal/currentRuntimeBridge.ts` as the single private
  core bridge for current-runtime constructor/types/history/method-sync helpers.
  `withPlate`, `withSlate`, `withStatic`, `PlateEditor`, `SlateEditor`,
  `BasePlugin`, `SlatePlugin`, `PlatePlugin`, `resolvePlugins`,
  `HistoryPlugin`, and `withSlate.spec.ts` now import the current-runtime
  surface from that bridge instead of `@platejs/slate-legacy` directly.
  `createPlateRuntimeEditor` now wraps runtime `inject.nodeProps` transforms in
  Plate element context so hook-backed navigation feedback can resolve the
  rendered element path on the Slate v2 runtime branch. The migration scanner
  artifact files were refreshed, and `hit-overrides.json` records the private
  bridge quarantine.
- Tests/oracles: core tests now catch the v2 runtime inject-context gap through
  `runs hook-backed createPlateEditor slate-v2 inject transformProps`; the
  previously failing row now passes and proves navigation highlight attributes
  render on the v2 runtime branch.
- Proof: `rg -n "from '@platejs/slate-legacy'" packages apps content docs
  --glob '!docs/plans/**'` reports only
  `packages/core/src/internal/currentRuntimeBridge.ts` and
  `packages/slate-legacy` type tests; `pnpm turbo typecheck
  --filter=./packages/core` passed; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core test` passed
  952 tests / 2316 assertions; `pnpm --filter @platejs/core build` passed;
  `node docs/plans/artifacts/plate-slate-v2-migration/scan-plate-slate-migration.mjs`
  passed with 5396 scanned files, 1 owner, 2649 hits, and 0 missing direct
  current Slate deps; `node
  docs/plans/artifacts/plate-slate-v2-migration/scan-plate-command-surface.mjs`
  passed with 313 rows across 30 owners; after warming `PORT=3100
  NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATE_BROWSER_PROOF=1 pnpm --filter www dev:slate`,
  `PLAYWRIGHT_BASE_URL=http://localhost:3100 pnpm --filter www
  test:slate-browser:chromium tests/slate-browser/playground.spec.ts` passed 1
  Chromium playground edit/undo/redo proof.
- Keep/revert/quarantine: keep. Direct imports are no longer scattered through
  public Plate code; the only direct core source import is a private bridge.
  Quarantine the bridge and `packages/core/package.json` dependency until the
  runtime/default-route packet replaces the current Plate editor contract.
- Deferred-with-owner: full Plate runtime/default-route migration and
  `packages/slate-legacy` deletion remain hard checkpoints. Do not expose this
  bridge as final API. Current declaration output still imports
  `@platejs/slate-legacy` because exported `PlateEditor.api` / `PlateEditor.tf`
  types are still the current Plate command facade; removing that requires the
  Plate v2 API cut, not source import cleanup.
- Workflow slowdown: the `@platejs/core` test script ignores the apparent file
  args and runs the package suite; this is acceptable proof here but should not
  be mistaken for a focused single-file command. The Playwright webServer path
  failed twice at `page.goto` because cold Next/Fumadocs route compile exceeded
  the 45s test timeout; manual warm-up showed `/blocks/playground` taking about
  71s and `/api/slate/ready` about 52s after restart, then the same browser row
  passed against the warmed server with `NEXT_PUBLIC_PLATE_BROWSER_PROOF=1`.
- Needs review: high. The source bridge is private, but generated declarations
  still expose the current legacy-backed Plate command facade because
  `PlateEditor.api/tf/getTransforms` are public today. I think this is the right
  temporary state for beta; pretending it can disappear before the Plate v2 API
  cut would be fake.
- Next owner: full Plate runtime/default-route checkpoint, not more import
  churn.

| What have I learned? | Core runtime is the real adapter checkpoint; fixture duplication should delegate to first-party Slate packages; structural type imports can move to v2 only when the runtime predicate/helper remains explicitly owned; root legacy methods should stay as local bridge types, not be added back to public editor contracts; plugin tx inference belongs in `PluginConfig` / `extendTx` / typed editor surfaces, not individual package generics; unparameterized base editors must stay non-recursive while `TSlateEditor`, `TPlateEditor`, and `PlateRuntimeEditor` carry installed-plugin tx inference; aggregate `platejs` imports are too ambiguous for migration specs, so package proofs should import editor helpers from the owning package; owner-import rewrites may raise visible scanner hit totals by making direct `@platejs/slate` imports countable; package tests can execute stale built core/aggregate output, so rebuild `@platejs/core` and sometimes `platejs` before treating module-resolution failures as product failures; runtime specs need the package plugin generic (`createPlateEditor<Value, typeof Plugin>`) when exercising non-core plugins |
| What have I done? | See Timeline and Packet ledger |
| Final closure state | Package-by-package migration lane is ready to close after autoreview: stale-symbol inventory is down to intentional `packages/slate-legacy`, command-surface candidates are classified, apps/www playground proof is green, and broad runtime/default-route work is a hard checkpoint instead of hidden remaining package cleanup. |

Open risks:
- Core runtime contract still depends on `@platejs/slate-legacy`; current inventory selection is closed down to the intentional scaffold, so the next owner is runtime/helper-boundary retirement or an explicit hard checkpoint. Core command-surface rows are classified, but broader runtime scaffold retirement remains open.
- `HistoryPlugin` now has a typed current-runtime bridge, but current Plate runtime history still depends on legacy `withHistory`; Slate v2 history is only proven on the v2 runtime path.
- `packages/slate-legacy` is green as a scaffold but cannot be deleted yet because core runtime/editor contracts still depend on current legacy editor/runtime semantics.
- Fresh first-party Chromium edit proof for `apps/www` playground now passes through the Slate browser harness over the current Plate proof adapter. Default Plate runtime routing remains the real hard checkpoint.
- `AnyPluginConfig` still intentionally uses broad top-type `any` fields; local `tx`-only hardening was rejected by core typecheck. Plate-side tx inference is now guarded by a type proof, but fully strict plugin carrier typing still requires a deliberate core plugin generic redesign, not a package migration cleanup packet.
